RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The two special portions of the sacrifice Pravargya and Upasada were duly observed; then the brahmins worshipped the gods with joy.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The illustrious sage performed certain rituals and offered Indra the part of the sacrifice due to him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Thereafter all partook of the soma-juice which destroys every sin.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The high-souled king duly undertook the third portion of the ceremony with the assistance of the holy brahmins.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	In the sacrifice, no oblation was omitted and none wrongly offered in the sacred fire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	All that was done was correctly carried out under the supervision of the sages.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	During the period of sacrifice, no brahmin experienced hunger or thirst.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Countless priests were present and each was attended by hundreds of disciples.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Workers, servants and other classes were feasted like the brahmins, and monks and ascetics were provided for abundantly.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The aged, the children, and the women were served with all they cared to eat, and those who attended on them were willing and pleasant.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	By the king's command, apparel, money and other gifts were freely distributed with immeasurable generosity.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Mountains of cooked and uncooked foods were to be seen and each could have what he required, to suit his needs.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Men and women from many lands were daily entertained with food and drink.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	From every side, the king heard the exclamations "How delicious is the food, we are well content".
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Servants and retainers gorgeously clad and wearing golden earrings, attended on the brahmins, while others adorned with jewels served other castes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	In the interval between the two parts of the sacrifice, eloquent and learned pundits debated metaphysical problems and vied with each other in the display of wisdom and acumen.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Day by day, the sacrificial ceremonies were carried out by learned and holy priests.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	There were none assisting at the holy ritual who were illiterate or unacquainted with the Vedas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Each attendant of the king was inspired by exalted principles and all were highly eloquent and deeply versed in the scriptures.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Eighteen pillars of wood were set up in the place of sacrifice, each made of a different kind of timber.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Priests, skilled in the art of sacrificial rites, overlaid them with gold.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Each of the eighteen columns was twenty-one feet in height, polished and of octangular shape and all were firmly fixed in the earth and covered with embroidered cloths.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	In addition, they were adorned with sandalwood and flowers and looked as beautiful as the constellation of the seven sages, in the sky.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Sacrificial pits were constructed by master masons and the fire kindled by brahmins.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The sacrificial pit prepared for King Dasaratha was formed like a great eagle in gold, its wings set with gems.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The beasts to be sacrificed to each particular deity were bound according to scriptural injunction.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	There were birds, snakes and horses, and according to tradition, the chief priest bound the aquatic animals, such as turtles, in the sacrificial pavilion.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Three hundred beasts and the horse which had roamed over the earth were assembled.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Queen Kaushalya joyfully paid reverence to the horse before making the sacrifice with three strokes of the sword.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Prompted by righteous desire, Queen Kaushalya passed the night watching over the dead body of the horse, then the priests caused the king's serving women and the courtesans to approach it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The twice-born of subdued senses cooked the fat of the horse on the fire in the manner prescribed by the shastra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	King Dasaratha inhaling the odour emitted by the fat, acknowledged and expiated his sins.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Sixteen assistant priests made offerings of parts of the horse into the fire, in spoons fashioned of cane, plaksha wood being used in other sacrifices.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	At the horse sacrifice, three days of special rituals are observed: during the first day the Agnistona is performed; during the second day, the Uktha rite, during the third day the Atiratra rite.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The great sacrificial acts named Jyotishtoma, Agnishtona, Atiratas, Abhijit, Vishnajit and Aptoryama are also observed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	King Dasaratha, the promoter of his dynasty, on the conclusion of the sacrifice, gave away four parts of his kingdom, as dakshina to the four priests.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The king distributed alms following the great example of Swayambhumanu of old.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The sacrifice being concluded, that great monarch gave large portions of the earth in charity, to the officiating priests, and finally that magnanimous sovereign bestowed the whole kingdom on the assisting priests.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Then the holy brahmins addressed that sinless monarch, saying: "O Lord of Men, we are not able to protect, defend and administer this vast empire, for we have dedicated ourselves to holy study.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Therefore, O Great King, we render back these lands to you, grant us in return some lesser gift, be it gems, gold or coins to help us in our hermitages."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Thus addressed by the learned brahmins, the king bestowed on them a hundred million pieces of gold, and four hundred million silver coins.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Then the assisting priests placed all the king's gifts before the holy sages, Vasishtha and Rishyasringa and begged them to distribute them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Each one received his just share and the priests were highly pleased and well satisfied.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The king gave away gold coins to those who had come to witness the sacrifice and ten million gold coins were bestowed on other brahmins present at that time.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	A needy mendicant begged for the diamond studded bracelet worn by the king himself and it was freely bestowed on him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Beholding the brahmins fully satisfied, King Dasaratha with great gladness made obeisance to them again and again.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The twice-born then bestowed their blessings on the king who was exceedingly liberal and valorous and who saluted them by prostrating himself on the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Thus ended the great sacrifice, the means of destroying sin and attaining heaven and scarcely to be accomplished by other monarchs.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	Then the king addressed Rishyasringa and said: "O You of great and virtuous resolve, tell me what further must be done by me to be blessed with an heir?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	14_The Ceremonies are performed with the appropriate rites	The Sage Rishyasringa replied: "O King, you shalt be blessed with four sons, who will perpetuate the royal line."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	The wise Rishyasringa, versed in the Scriptures, meditated for a while and then spoke to King Dasaratha saying:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	"O King, I will perform the sacrifice Puttatresti, spoken of in the Atharva Veda, which will assist you in your endeavour to obtain a son."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	Then the sage inaugurated the sacrifice and poured oblations into the sacred fire accompanied by the chant of Vedic mantras.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	The celestial beings, gandharvas, siddhas and sages assembled to obtain their portion of the sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	After the sacrifice, they all approached Shri Brahma, the Lord of mankind and with joined palms addressed him:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	They said: "O Blessed Lord, having been favoured by you, the Asura Ravana, perpetually troubles us who are helpless, since you have granted great boons to him and we are forced to bear his fearful oppression.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	"This Lord of Rakshasas has persecuted the three worlds and having overthrown the guardians of the earth, he has even humbled Indra himself.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	Provoking the sages, contemplatives, brahmins and the gods, he even controls the sun's rays and the wind's power, even the ocean in his presence is still.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	At his approach, O Blessed Lord, we are terrified.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	O Giver of Boons, be pleased to bring about his destruction."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	Hearing these words, Brahma reflected for a while and answered: "I have devised a plan for slaying this wicked tyrant.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	It was granted to Ravana that no gandharva, yaksha or deva should be able to slay him, but thinking man to be of no account, he did not ask to be made invulnerable in regard to him; therefore, none but man can destroy him."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	These words, uttered by Shri Brahma filled the celestial and other beings with joy.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	At this time the immortal Vishnu, with conch, disc and mace, the Overlord of the whole world, clad in a yellow robe, appeared at that place.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	Adored by the gods, he drew near and took his seat by Shri Brahma, then all the gods addressed him saying:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	"O Madhusudana, for the good of all beings, we entreat You, to be born as heir to the supremely righteous, charitable and illustrious Sage Dasaratha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	Appear, O Lord, in the form of four sons to the three consorts of that great king.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	Descending into a human body, do you slay Ravana, the scourge of the universe, whom we are unable to destroy.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	That ignorant Ravana, by his power, afflicts the devas, siddhas and sages.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	O Lord, that wicked asura, sporting in the garden of Indra, has slain countless nymphs and gandharvas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	In company with the sages, we approach You so that we may be released from this oppression.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	We take refuge in You, You are our only asylum!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	O Lord, we beseech You to take birth as man in order to destroy the enemy of men and gods."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	Thus did the gods appeal to Shri Vishnu and He, adored by the world, answered them who had taken refuge in Him:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	"O Devas, fear no more, peace be with you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	For your sake, I will destroy Ravana, together with his sons, grandsons, counsellors, friends and relatives.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	Having slain that cruel and wicked asura, the cause of fear to the divine sages, I will rule in the world of mortals for eleven thousand years."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	Thus did Shri Vishnu grant a boon to the gods, and then reflected as to where on the earth he should take birth as man.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	Then the lotus-eyed Lord resolved to become incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	The celestial sages, the heavenly musicians and the nymphs praised the Lord saying: "O Universal Sovereign, destroy the wicked asura, who is arrogant, powerful and vain, the enemy of Indra and the scourge of the ascetics and pious men, one who strikes terror into every heart, causing universal lamentation.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	15_To destroy Ravana, Shri Vishnu resolves to incarnate	"Destroy, O Lord, this mighty being, together with his army, generals, relatives, friends and followers, remove the cause of the world's woe and then return to your perfect abode."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	The Omniscient Lord, Shri Narayana, listened to the praise offered by the gods and honouring them, uttered words of pleasing import to them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	He said: "O Devas, by what means may the King of the Asuras be slain, that thorn in the side of holy men?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	The gods with one accord answered the imperishable Lord, crying: "Do You become incarnate in the form of man and slay him in open fight.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	O Conqueror of Your foes, Ravana has long practised austerities, by means of which he has won the favour of the world-revered Brahma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	That deity has granted him a boon, by which he is rendered invulnerable to all but man.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Considering man of no account, he does not fear him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	The boon bestowed on him by Shri Brahma has made him arrogant and he is bringing destruction to the three worlds and carrying off women by violence.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Therefore, O Lord, man alone can bring about his death."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Hearing the words of the gods, Shri Vishnu resolved to choose King Dasaratha as his sire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	At that time, the illustrious King Dasaratha, the slayer of his foes, began to observe the sacrifice in order to obtain an heir.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Shri Vishnu, having formed his resolution to appear in human form and concluded his deUberations with Shri Brahma, vanished.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Forthwith there issued from King Dasaratha's sacrificial fire to the sound resembling the beating of a drum, a great Being of limitless splendour, of glowing countenance, clad in red and hairy as a lion.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Bearing auspicious marks and adorned with beautiful ornaments, his height was equal to the peak of a mountain.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Striding boldly like a lion, his form shone as fire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	In both hands he carried, as would a beloved spouse, a vessel of gold, with a silver cover, filled with payasa.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	This great Being addressed the king saying: "O King, I come from Prajapati.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	The king bowing down with joined palms, answered: "You are welcome, O Lord, what orders hast you for me?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Then the Being replied: "Receive the fruit of your sacrifice!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	O Chief of Men, accept this dish of payasa prepared by the gods, it will bring you sons and increase your power.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Let it be eaten by your consorts, they will then present you with the heirs for whose sake you have performed the sacrifice."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	The king received the food contained in the golden vessel prepared by the gods and reverently raised it to his forehead.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Having received the divine repast, he rejoiced as a penniless man on obtaining wealth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Forthwith that wonderful and resplendent being vanished, having offered the consecrated food to the king.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	The tidings of this great event caused the consorts of King Dasaratha extreme delight and they appeared as radiant as the beams of the moon irradiating the autumnal sky.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Entering the private apartments, the king addressed Queen Kaushalya, saying: "Receive this food and partake of it that you mayest have a son."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Thereafter, the monarch gave half of the dish to Queen Kaushalya and one-third to Queen Sumitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Then he gave the eighth of the payasa to Queen Kaikeyi and, after reflection, the remainder to Queen Sumitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	In this way, the King divided the dish of payasa among his three queens.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	On partaking of the food, the beautiful queens were overjoyed and considered themselves most fortunate.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	Having consumed the payasa presented to them by the king, the queens soon became pregnant, their wombs glowing like the fire in the sun.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	16_Shri Vishnu decides to incarnate as the four sons of King Dasaratha	The illustrious sovereign perceiving that the wombs of his consorts were quickened and that his great desire was about to be fulfilled, was filled with supreme joy, as is Shri Vishnu when worshipped by the gods and perfect beings in the celestial region.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	When the sacrifice of King Dasaratha had been brought to a successful conclusion, the gods, receiving their due portions, returned to their abode.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The king also, having fulfilled the obligations incurred by his initiation, returned to the capital with his queens, servants, army and vehicles.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The royal guests to whom due hospitality had been shown, made obeisance to the Sage Vasishtha and returned to their homes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	When they departed, ornaments, apparel and gifts were distributed to their armies who set out for their own cities with joy.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	King Dasaratha attended the departure of his guests and then re-entered the capital in a procession preceded by the holy brahmins.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Rishyasringa with his wife Shanta then took leave of the monarch and departed to his own city, King Dasaratha accompanying him for some distance.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Then the king, expecting to be blessed with an heir, dwelt happily in Ayodhya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Six seasons after the completion of the sacrifice, in the twelfth month, on the ninth day of the moon of Caitramas, the star Punarvasu was in the ascendant, and the planets, the Sun, Mars, Saturn, Jupiter and Venus were exalted, and those signs of the zodiac, such as the Ram, the Fishes, and the Scales in auspicious aspects, the moon and Jupiter being in conjunction at the period called Karka.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Then the world-honoured Lord of the World, endowed with divine attributes, Shri Ramacandra was born of the womb of Kaushalya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The Promoter of the glory of the House of Ikshvaku, the blessed Lord Vishnu was born as a son of Queen Kaushalya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	When this child of limitless splendour was born, the queen looked most beautiful, like Aditi of old, favoured by Indra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The hero of the realm of truth, Bharata, was born of Queen Kaikeyi.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Possessed of every grace, he was endowed with a quarter of the glory of Shri Vishnu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Sumitra gave birth to Lakshmana and Shatrughna, heroes skilful in the wielding of weapons and also partaking of Shri Vishnu's glory.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Bharata was born when the star Pushya was in the ascendant in the Lagna Meena.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	During the ascendance of the star Shlasa in the Lagna Karka, at the time of sunrise Shatrughna was born.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Each of the sons of the king had special attributes and were endowed with great qualities, they were as resplendent as the Purva, Uttara and Bhadripata stars.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	At that time gandharvas played divine melodies, nymphs danced, celestial drums were heard and the gods showered flowers from the sky.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Everywhere in the capital, signs of rejoicing were apparent; the streets were filled with actors and dancers and those who sang or played on various instruments.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The king gave gifts to the bards and ballad singers and conferred wealth and cows on the brahmins.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The four children were named on the twelfth day; the eldest son received the name Ramacandra, and the name given to the son of Queen Kaikeyi was Bharata.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The sons of Queen Sumitra were called Lakshmana and Shatrughna.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The ceremony was performed by the holy Sage Vasishtha with great joy.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	After this, the brahmins of the capital and the country were feasted and presented with gifts and precious gems.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Resembling the deity Shri Brahma, the king showed universal benevolence.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The princes grew in the knowledge of the Veda, in courage and active goodwill to all.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Though each was wise, learned and possessed of every virtue, yet Shri Ramacandra excelled them in truthfulness and energy, and was beloved of all, like the flawless orb of the moon.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Expert in mounting the elephant, the horse and the chariot, he was skilful in archery and devoted to the service of his parents.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Shri Lakshmana cherished an exceeding love for his elder brother Shri Ramacandra, the delight of the world, and Shri Rama loved him also as his very self.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Shri Ramacandra loved Lakshmana who was endowed with every excellent quality, as his own life, and neither slept nor partook of any nourishment without the other.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	When Raghava mounted on horseback, engaged in the chase, Shri Lakshmana followed with bow and arrows to protect him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Emulating the example of Shri Ramacandra, Bharata loved Shatrughna and was loved by him with equal affection.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The monarch was as pleased and satisfied with his four sons as is Shri Brahma with the four Vedas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Observing the wisdom, prudence and modesty of his children, who were endowed with every great attribute, King Dasaratha derived as great a delight from them as Brahma from the four guardians of the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The princes studied the Veda with perseverance, affectionately attended on the king and acquired proficiency in the use of arms.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	One day when the illustrious sovereign was in council with his relatives, ministers, and learned preceptors, deliberating on the marriage of his four sons, the great Sage Vishvamitra appeared in the capital.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Seeking an audience with the king, he addressed the doorkeeper, saying: "Inform the king speedily that the son of Gadhi of the race of Kaushika is at the gate."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The awe-stricken guard hastened to the royal apartment and conveyed the tidings with due respect to his majesty, who with his Guru Vasishtha went forth to welcome the sage at the gate and bring him into the royal palace.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	As Brahma welcomes Indra, so did they greet the muni, and beholding that resplendent and mighty ascetic, the observer of great vows, of cheerful countenance, the king offered him arghya according to the prescribed tradition.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	The virtuous Vishvamitra then enquired of the king concerning the welfare of the empire, the prosperity of his people, relatives and friends and also as to the state of the royal treasury.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Thereafter, the sage questioned the monarch further, saying: "Are your vassals obedient to you?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Are thine enemies subdued?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Are the Vedic sacrifices duly observed in your dominion?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Are strangers entertained with fitting hospitality?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Then after enquiring as to the well-being of Shri Vasishtha and other sages, Shri Vishvamitra entered the palace.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Here the king once more paid him reverence and with delight addressed him saying: "O August Sage, your coming has caused me as great a joy as the acquisition of ambrosia or the advent of rain falling on the parched earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	O Sage, your approach is as grateful to me as the birth of a son to one without an heir or the recovery of his wealth to one who imagined it to be irretrievably lost.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	O Mighty Sage, I welcome you with my whole heart, say what commands you have for me?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	When your glance does fall upon me, O Sage, I become righteous and acquire merit; to-day my life is rendered fruitful and the purpose of my birth is accomplished since you have visited me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	O Auspicious One, formerly you wast a warrior sage, illustrious by virtue of your sacred practices, but now you are become a brahmin and art worthy of supreme worship by me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Thine advent has conferred purity and blessing on me, and by your sacred presence both the kingdom and I have been purged of every offence.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Be pleased to tell us of the purpose of your coming, I desire to manifest my gratitude to you by rendering you service.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	O Kaushika, do not hesitate to speak your will, I am ready to do anything for you; you are to me as a god.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	O Brahman Seer, by beholding you, I have acquired the great merits of a pilgrimage."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_King Dasaratha's sons are born and grow to manhood	Hearing the words of King Dasaratha, sweet sounding and in accordance with the scriptural injunctions, the great sage, the repository of all excellent qualities, was highly gratified.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	Shri Vishnu having become the sons of King Dasaratha, the divine Brahma thus addressed the gods: "The blessed Lord Vishnu, the Ocean of Truth is engaged in a just undertaking for the good of all, you should therefore support Him by becoming incarnate as great beings in the monkey tribe, skilled in the arts of magic, swift as the wind, conversant with the dictates of virtue, wise and equal in might to the Lord, invincible, endowed with celestial bodies and skilful in the science of warfare.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	Some among you should assume the forms of nymphs, gandharvas and female ascetics who will give birth to heroes in the monkey tribe.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	"In the past, when I yawned, the great bear, by the name of Jambavan, issued from my mouth."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	The gods thus instructed by the blessed Lord, caused warriors to be born in the monkey tribe from the wombs of countless celestial beings.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	Indra created Bali, the Sun created Sugriva; Brihaspati created the wise Tara, Kuvera begat Gandhamadana, Vishakarma begat the mighty ape Nala, Agni begat Nila, who was as resplendent as fire and in valour surpassed his father.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	The Asvini-Kumaras produced Minda and Dvivida; Varuna begat Suchena; Megha, was the father of Sharabha, the mighty; Pavana begat the warrior called Hanuman, whose body was as hard as a diamond and whose speed equalled an eagle's; he excelled all the other warriors in wisdom and power.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	There were thousands of warriors born in the monkey tribe ready to destroy Ravana.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	All the bears, monkeys and chimpanzees resembled the god that had produced them in characteristics, habits and prowess, and many were of outstanding valour.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	The female chimpanzees and bears gave birth to great beings of divine nature.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	They produced hundreds and thousands of healthy progeny.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	These dwellers of the forest were imposing in form and in strength and fearlessness resembled lions and tigers.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	All were able to cleave rocks and mountains and fight with their nails and teeth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	Skilled in every kind of weapon, they could shake great peaks, uproot the stoutest trees and by their velocity even put the sea god to shame.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	Able to tear up the earth with their feet and cause the ocean to overflow, they could fly in the air and even seize the clouds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	These beings of the monkey tribe wandered in the woods, making captive the elephants, and by their shouts causing the birds in flight to fall to the ground.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	Thus were born millions of monkeys, able to assume any form, together with hundreds and thousands of monkey chiefs.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	These chiefs begot other brave and powerful beings, some of whom dwelt on the mountains while others inhabited the valleys and forests.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	The two brothers, Sugriva, the offspring of Surya, and Bali, the son of Indra, became the leaders of all the monkeys.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	Others lived under the command of group leaders, such as Nala, Nila and Hanuman.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	They were as strong as eagles and skilled in every sort of warfare.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	Wandering about the forest, they slew lions, tigers and poisonous snakes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	The powerful long-armed Bali protected the monkeys, bears and chimpanzees by his prowess.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	17_To assist Shri Vishnu, celestial beings incarnate as warriors of the monkey tribe	These heroes, invincible as mountains and of immense size, born to assist Shri Rama, filled the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	Hearing the laudatory and admirable words of that Lion among lungs, Dasaratha, the great Sage Vishvamitra answered: "O Great King, who in the world save one of the House of Ikshvaku, instructed by Shri Vasishtha, could give tongue to such utterances?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	O Illustrious Monarch, I will now unfold my purpose, do you fulfil it and prove the truth of your words.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	"O Chief of Men, when I undertake the observance of sacred sacrifices to enhance my perfection, two rakshasas, adepts in magic, create great impediments.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	When, after long effort, the sacrifice approaches consummation, then these two rakshasas, Marica and Suvahu destroy the rite and defile the altar with blood and flesh.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	My holy endeavours being thus frustrated, I become despondent and leave the place of sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	O King, it is not permitted to me to show wrath when engaged in sacrifice, and I therefore refrain from cursing them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	Do you lend me the services of your son, Shri Ramacandra, the truthful, the brave, that hero, whose locks fall on his cheeks.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	"Under my protection, he will destroy those mischievous rakshasas and I will confer great blessings on him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	I will instruct him for his good in many sciences and he will become famous in the three worlds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	The rakshasas will not be able to stand against Rama and no one else can destroy them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	They are proud and powerful, but now, owing to their sins, their destruction is imminent, they will not be able to withstand Shri Ramacandra,
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	"Do not allow a father's affection to overcome you; I assure you that in the presence of Shri Ramacandra, the rakshasas are as good as slain.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	Rama's virtues are known to Shri Vasishtha and other ascetics.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	O King, if you seeks everlasting renown and merit in this world, then let Shri Rama go with me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	Seek the advice of Shri Vasishtha and your counsellors and if they approve the project, give me Ramacandra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	Be pleased, O King, to give up your beloved son for the space of ten days, so that I may complete the sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	O King, help me in furthering my sacrifice, and do not let the allotted time pass in vain.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	Do what is auspicious, do not grieve."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	The upright and resplendent Sage Vishvamitra having uttered these righteous words, became silent.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	The words of Shri Vishvamitra filled the king with anxiety and he became distraught.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	19_Vishvamitra's request	Because of these inexorable words, the monarch trembled and fell unconscious from his seat overcome with grief.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	For some time the king lay insensible, then regaining consciousness he said: "My lotus-eyed Rama is but fifteen years old, I cannot believe he is capable of contending with the rakshasas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	I possess a large and well-equipped army and will myself lead it against the demons.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	My seasoned warriors, who are courageous and skilled in bearing weapons and who are suitably remunerated by me, are fit to fight the rakshasas in battle; therefore, do not ask for Rama.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	I myself, bearing my bow and arrows, will lead the army in the field and fight to my last breath.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	With this protection, your sacrifice will come to a successful conclusion.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	I will go thither in person, do not take away Shri Ramacandra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	Shri Rama is still a child without military experience, he cannot estimate the strength or weakness of the enemy, he has not yet acquired proficiency in warfare.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	"You knowest well, O Sage, how crafty are the rakshasas in combat.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	Shri Ramacandra is not capable of opposing them successfully.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	I cannot bear the thought of Ramacandra contending with them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	O Sage, I shall not five, even for a moment, if Shri Rama be separated from me, therefore, I entreat you, do not ask for him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	Should'st you insist on Rama accompanying you, then take my forces also with you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	O August Vishvamitra, recollect I pray you that I am now nine thousand years old and have begotten these sons with great difficulty.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	These princes are dearer to me than life itself and Shri Ramacandra is the dearest of them all.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	Excelling in virtue, he is my eldest son, therefore, do not take him from me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	O Great Sage, how powerful are these rakshasas?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	Who are their supporters and how dost you imagine Shri Rama can destroy them?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	O Blessed Lord, say if you deemest that I and my army may successfully oppose those rakshasas who are skilled in magic?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	Shri Vishvamitra answered: "O King, Ravana, born of the great family of Paulastya, having been favoured by Brahma with a boon, is oppressing the three worlds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	He is exceedingly powerful and supported by many asuric followers.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	It is said that this great warrior Ravana is the King of Asuras.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	He is the brother of Kuvera and the son of the Sage Vishravas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	He does not obstruct the lesser sacrifices in person, but two mighty rakshasas named Marica and Suvahu, prompted by him, disrupt the sacrificial rites."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	The king listened to the muni's words and then spoke: "I am not able to oppose that evil-souled asura.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	O Knower of the Law of Righteousness, I am but a wretched man and you are worthy of my worship; you are verily a god and also my spiritual preceptor.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	Since the gods, the danavas, gand-harvas, yakshas, birds and snakes cannot destroy Ravana, how can man do so?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	In battle, Ravana is able to defeat the mightiest warriors, it is certain therefore, that neither I nor my army can*ontend with him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	How can I then send my son, beautiful as a god, but inexperienced in war, to oppose Ravana?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	O Sage, I will not let my young child go.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	Lavana, the son of Madhu is among those who destroy the sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	I will not give up my son.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	The sons of Sunda and Upasunda, Marica and Suvahu, who resemble death itself in battle, are among those who impede the sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	They are skilful and seasoned warriors, I dare not send my young son against them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	Whoever you chooses, friends, relatives or even I myself will accompany you to engage in the fight."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	On hearing the king's injudicious words, the holy sage was enraged.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	20_Dasarathas reluctance to allow Shri Rama to contend with Marica and Suvahu	As an oblation poured into the fire adds to the fierceness of the flame, so did the words of King Dasaratha add to the fire of anger kindled in the sage's heart.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Hearing the words of King Dasaratha inspired by solicitude for his son, the great sage replied in displeasure:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	"O King, recollect that you are born in the house of Raghu, how can'st you presume to break your promise?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	This action is unworthy of your royal line and is also improper.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	If this be your determined desire, I will take my leave, do you live at ease amidst your relatives and friends, O Violater of your Word!"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	At the wrath of the august sage, the whole earth shook and the gods began to tremble.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Seeing the whole world shaken with terror, the wise and patient muni Shri Vasishtha intervened, and thus addressed the king:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	"O King, you are born in the family of Ikshvaku and art righteousness personified!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Blessed by fortune, filled with patience and endurance, you have cherished great vows and should'st not, therefore, abandon dharma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	The three worlds know you as virtuous, it is your duty to maintain integrity and not to act in contradiction to it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	O Chief of Men, if one making a promise does not honour it, he loses the merit of his good deeds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	It is, therefore, for you to be faithful to your word and let Rama accompany this sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Though Shri Ramacandra is inexperienced in warfare, yet the asuras will not be able to overcome him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Furthermore, he is under the protection of Shri Vishvamitra and no harm can come to him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	How can one steal the nectar that is surrounded by fire?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	The holy Vish-wamitra is virtue itself, his powers are unsurpassed, and there is none living equal to him in wisdom and asceticism.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	In the whole world of men and other beings, none excels him in the use of weapons and none has fathomed the depth of his nature.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Neither the celestials, nor the sages, nor the asuras, nor any other beings know the full glory of this sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	The god Krishasawa and his highly virtuous sons gave every variety of weapon to Vishvamitra when he was king.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	The two daughters of Daksha, Jaya and Suprabha invented thousands of resplendent weapons.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Shri Vishvamitra is not one, but many in one form; he is illustrious, mighty and able to defeat any in battle.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Jaya produced five hundred weapons supremely potent and capable of destroying a host of asuras.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Suprabha also created five hundred weapons of war which no foe in the world could withstand.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Shri Vishvamitra is an adept in the use of all these arms, O King, he is also able to create many new weapons and there is nothing in the three divisions of time which is not known to him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	Do not hesitate to send your son Rama with this mighty and courageous sage, Shri Vishvamitra, and do not entertain any fears for his safety.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	The Sage Vishvamitra is well able to destroy the demons, but asks for the services of your son for his own good."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	21_Vishvamitra's request	The Guru Vasishtha having thus exhorted the monarch, the king cheerfully acquiesced to Shri Ramacandra accompanying the sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	Instructed by Shri Vasishtha, King Dasaratha with a cheerful countenance sent for Prince Rama and also Prince Lakshmana.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	At the time of their departure, the Peace Chant was recited by the king, whilst the Guru Vasishtha pronounced the benediction.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	The illustrious sovereign then smelt the heads of his sons with joy and delivered them into the care of the sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	When the lotus-eyed Ramacandra and Prince Lakshmana had taken their leave, Vayu sent forth cool and gentle breezes redolent with fragrance and the celestial beings showered down flowers, to the sound of the beating of drums and the blowing of conches.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	Shri Vishvamitra led the way followed by the most illustrious Ramacandra, then came Shri Lakshmana of flowing locks, bearing a bow in his hand.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	The two handsome and powerful princes with quivers on their backs and bows in their hands, adding lustre to the ten cardinal points, followed the muni as if two three-headed snakes were following Shri Vishvamitra or as the Asvinikumaras and Kinneras follow Brahma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	Shri Ramacandra and Lakshmana, armed with their bows, adorned with precious jewels and wearing gloves made of deerskin, resplendent and beautiful, girt with swords, following the holy sage, looked like the two sons of Shiva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	Coming to the river Sarayu, nine miles to the south of the capital, the Sage Vishvamitra addressed Shri Rama in gentle accents, saying: "O Child, purify your body with water.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	When you have done so, I will teach you the use of Bala and Atibala.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	The application of these two herbs will prevent you from being fatigued or suffering from disease, nor will age affect you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	Even should'st you retire to rest without performing the purification ceremony no demon will be able to afflict you; none in the world will equal you in prowess.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	O Rama, no one in the three worlds will rival you in good fortune, skill, knowledge and practical wisdom.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	O Prince, when you have learnt these sciences, you will be able to answer any question and you will be unique in scholarship.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	These two sciences, O Rama, are the parents of all other sciences.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	You will be able to control hunger and thirst by their application.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	O Prince of the House of Raghu, by the mastery of this lore, Bala and Atibala, you will attain renown throughout the whole world.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	These brilliant sciences are the daughters of Brahma, I shall impart them to you, O Prince, because you are qualified to receive them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	O Rama, all the fruits of this knowledge are already your attributes, yet when you have mastered it, you will be able to teach it to others."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	Shri Ramacandra then poured the water over his body and with a cheerful countenance said to the Sage Vishvamitra:--"O Great Rishi, I am your servant, teach me these sciences."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	Possessed of the knowledge of these two sciences, the mighty Rama resembled the sun in autumn, emitting a thousand rays.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	Then the two brothers massaged the feet of the holy Guru and passed the night pleasantly on the banks of the river Sarayu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	22_Ramachandra and Lakshmana set forth with Vishvamitra	Shri Rama being unaccustomed to sleeping on the ground, the two sons of King Dasaratha made a bed of grass, then having listened to the gentle words of Shri Vishvamitra, they passed the night in sleep.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	A little before dawn, the great Muni Vishvamitra, reclining on his grassy couch, addressed the princes, saying: "O Son of Queen Kaushalya, O Rama, the dawn is about to break, arise and perform your morning devotions."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	The two princes, hearing the words of the most generous sage, rose, performed their ablutions, offered ceremonial water to the rising sun, worshipped their ancestors and began to repeat the holy Gayatri.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	Their devotions completed, they offered salutations with great reverence to the distinguished ascetic and stood ready to proceed further.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	In their company, the holy sage reached the confluence of the rivers where the Ganges unites herself with the Sarayu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	There they beheld the holy ascetics in their sacred hermitage, where for a long time they had practised Yoga assiduously.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	Seeing the peaceful hermitage, Shri Ramacandra and Lakshmana were filled with delight and said to the Sage Vishvamitra: "O Blessed Lord, whose holy hermitage is this?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	Who dwells here?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	We are both eager to hear of this."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	The great sage smiled and answered Rama, saying: "Hear, my son, I will tell you who formerly dwelt here.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	Kandarpa, whom the pundits called Kama once took human form and fixed in meditation, worshipped the Lord Shiva here.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	When Shri Shiva was passing with his newly-wedded bride, accompanied by celestial beings, Kama tried to agitate the mind of the Lord Shiva and reaped the due punishment of his insolence.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	O Son of the House of Raghu, Shiva in wrath opened his third eye and the members of Kama's body were consumed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	Since Kama was reduced to ashes by the God, he has been a disembodied being.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	O Rama, since that time, he has been known as Ananga (bodiless) and the country where his limbs were strewn as he sought to flee, is known as Anga.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	This hermitage belongs to the Lord Shiva and the holy men who dwell here are his traditional devotees: they are both righteous and sinless.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	O Rama, You of pleasing looks, this night I shall break my journey at this hermitage and to-morrow we shall cross the sacred river and proceed further.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	O Rama, let us first purify ourselves by bathing and then recite the holy Gayatri silently, offering oblations into the sacred fire, we will thereafter pass the night in the hermitage."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	While Shri Rama and the sage were conversing, the holy ascetics dwelling in the hermitage, knew by the power of their Yoga, that these great beings were approaching and were highly gratified.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	Having presented arghya to Shri Vishvamitra, they then offered hospitality to Shri Ramacandra and Lakshmana.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	23_Ramachandra and Lakshmana reach the hermitage of Kama	Entertained by those dwelling in the hermitage who regaled them with the holy traditions and philosophical discourses, they remained there for their evening devotion and with great delight abode in the hermitage of Kama, the devout sages gathering round Shri Vishvamitra who engaged them in pleasing converse.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	When the day dawned, the two princes performed their daily devotions and followed Shri Vishvamitra to the river.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	The keepers of sacred vows, the dwellers in the holy hermitage accompanied them to the river bank and arranged for an excellent boat to take them across; they said to Shri Vishvamitra:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	"O Great Rishi, do not delay, please board the vessel with the royal princes, now, and thus avoid the heat of the day."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	Shri Vishvamitra paid reverence to the devout sages and proceeded to cross the sacred river.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	When the craft was in mid-stream, the roar of the waters was heard by Shri Ramacandra and his younger brother.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	They questioned the holy sage, saying: "O Venerable Lord, what is the cause of this tumult?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	In answer to Shri Ramacandra, Shri Vishvamitra described the cause of the sound in the following manner:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	"O Prince, on Mount Kailasha, Shri Brahma created a lake by the power of his thought, on account of which it is called the Lake of the Mind (Manasarovara).
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	The holy river Sarayu rises in the Manasa Lake and flows through the capital Ayodhya, here it joins the sacred stream Gunga, and this sound is produced when the two rivers unite.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	With concentrated mind, offer salutations to them."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	The two royal princes made obeisance to the rivers, and having reached the southern bank, left the boat and proceeded onward.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	Walking further, the two princes beheld a dark and terrible forest and Shri Ramacandra again addressed the Sage as follows: "O Great Sage, this forest looks dark and sinister; above the ceaseless clamour of crickets and other insects, fearful beasts can be heard roaring.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	The forest resounds with their dread cries while the harsh and discordant notes of birds echo through it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	See, O Sage!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	Boars, lions, tigers and elephants abound there, it is overgrown with dhara, ashvakama, kujaja, patala, sillea and tinduka trees, it is indeed terrifying."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	The highly resplendent Sage Vishvamitra hearing these words, said: "My son, I will tell you something of this dark forest.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	Formerly there were two cities named Malava and Karusha, they were both prosperous and resembled the cities built by the gods.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	O Rama, in ancient times, Indra slew the wicked Vritrasura then, being hungry and thirsty, he went to an inauspicious and isolated place where he became distressed on account of the sin of having slain a brahmin.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	The gods and holy sages bathed Indra in the sacred waters of the Ganges, and purged away his sin by pouring jars of water charged with mantrams over him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	In this way, the remorse of Indra was appeased, the pollution caused by slaying a brahmin was washed away and he was highly gratified.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	Purified and sinless, Indra gladly conferred a boon on this land saying: 'These two cities will be known as Malava and Karusha and they will acquire great renown, their prosperity will be famed throughout the earth.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	"When Indra thus favoured these two cities, the celestial beings praised him and cried: 'Be it so.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	These two places soon enjoyed great prosperity and fame.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	In the course of time, a perverse yakshini was born here, possessing the strength of a thousand elephants.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	Her name was Taraka, the wife of Sunda, and her son was the rakshasa, Marica, who was equal in strength to Indra himself.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	He possessed long arms, an enormous mouth, and a gigiantic body.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	This terrible rakshasa continually destroys the people of these two lands.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	"O Rama, the wicked Taraka constantly plunders and devastates these two countries.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	Obstructing the road, she lives at two miles distance from here; let us enter the forest of Taraka.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	By my command, O Rama, do you slay the wicked yakshini and set the country free.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	O Rama, none dares to come hither for fear of Taraka; save this land from the dangerous demoness.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	This is why this forest is uninhabited, but you can'st restore it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	24_The two princes with Vishvamitra behold the dark forest of Taraka	This wicked yakshini is unceasingly bent on her evil designs."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	Hearing the words of Shri Vishvamitra, Shri Rama of limitless power and influence uttered the following auspicious words:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	"O Great Sage, it is said that the yakshinis have little power, then how is it that Taraka has come to possess the strength of a thousand elephants?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	The mahatma listened to Rama's words and said: "O Prince, I will relate the story to you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	This female demon has acquired her great strength by virtue of a boon which she received.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	In the past, a powerful yaksha by the name of Suketu, who was virtuous but childless, performed many yogic practices which pleased Shri Brahma, who promised him a daughter by name Taraka, and conferred on her the strength of a thousand elephants.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	But the most illustrious Brahma did not grant a son to that yaksha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	When the daughter grew up and possessed both the charm of youth and great beauty, her father gave her in marriage to Sunda, the son of Jambha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	After some time, the yakshini gave birth to a son.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	His name was Marica and he was very powerful; though born of yaksha parentage he became a rakshasa through a curse.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	O Rama, when the Sage Agastya condemned Sunda to death by cursing him, then Taraka and her son wished to devour the sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	Seeing her running towards him, the blessed Sage Agastya cursed Marica and said 'Become a demon'.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	He also cursed that wicked woman so that she became a cannibal with a hideous countenance.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	Shri Agastya said: * May your beauty vanish and mayest you become a terrible rakshasi.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	Then Taraka, transported with anger under this curse, began to destroy this sacred land because it was here that the Sage Agastya performed his yogic practices.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	"O Rama, you must slay this wicked and impious demon Taraka, who ravages the land.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	For the good of die brahmins and the king, O Raghava, accomplish this; do not hesitate to destroy this vile yakshini.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	It is the duty of a warrior to protect those of the four castes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	A prince must not eschew deeds that are painful and difficult, for the preservation of his people.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	It is according to the law of eternal dharma, O Rama, that even deeds that appear ruthless, are permitted to those appointed to protect their subjects.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	O Raghava, Taraka is wholly evil, and therefore must be destroyed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	It is said that in the past Manthara, a daughter of King Virocana, was slain by Indra because she was the cause of the destruction of others.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	The blessed Lord Vishnu Himself slew the wife of the Sage Bhrigu, devoted to her husband, and the mother of Shukra because she was intent on killing Indra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	Many other great-souled princes of old also condemned wicked women to death.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	25_Vishvamitra seeks to convince Rama that it is his duty to slay Taraka	Therefore, it is for you to fulfil your duty and slay this yakshini without delay."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	The son of Dasaratha, firm in his vows, listened to the inspiring words of the Sage Vishvamitra, which filled him with ardour, and with joined palms he humbly addressed him:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	"To fulfil the commands of my royal sire and to honour his promise, I deem it my duty to act according to your instructions without hesitation.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	My father, the emperor, at the time of my departure from Ayodhya bade me carry out your injunctions--O Muni, I shall honour them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	I am prepared to execute your commands, O Rishi, because it will lead to the benefit of the brahmins and the king, and will also bring happiness to the people of this land."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Having spoken thus, Shri Rama grasped his bow and, twanging the string, filled all the cardinal points with the sound.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	The denizens of the forest were terrified, and Taraka was overcome with helpless rage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Full of wrath that yakshini ran in the direction from which the sound came and Shri Ramacandra beholding that gigantic and misshapen monster was incensed and said to Lakshmana: "O Brother, behold this fearful yakshini of formidable size, whose veiy aspect would strike terror into timorous hearts.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	See, O Lakshmana, how I shall cut off her ears and nose and put her to flight!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	She is horrible, versed in black magic and hard to subdue, but it is not proper to deprive a woman of her life.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	A woman is worthy of protection, therefore, I shall incapacitate her, by depriving her of the power of motion thus preventing her from doing further mischief."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	While Shri Rama was still speaking, the dreadful Taraka ran towards him roaring with uplifted arms.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	The Rishi Vishvamitra approaching her encouraged Rama, with a shout, crying, "Jai to the descendant of Raghu".
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Notwithstanding, Taraka raised a thick cloud of dust and for a while Shri Rama and Lakshmana could see nothing.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Then the yakshini by the power of magic caused a shower of rocks to rain on the two brothers and Rama was now filled with wrath.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Parrying the rain of rocks and advancing towards her, he cut off both her hands.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Then Shri Lakshmana severed the nose and ears of the asuri who had already been deprived of her hands.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Assuming various forms, she tried to deceive the princes by vanishing away.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Then from her hiding place, she showered heavy rocks on them, and a rain of stones fell on every side.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Shri Vishvamitra, who stood watching the combat, now cried: "Enough, she does not deserve further mercy; should'st you spare her, she will gain strength through her magic powers and will again break up our holy rites.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	The evening is approaching and in the evening rakshasas are overcome with difficulty; slay her, therefore, without delay."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Then Shri Vishvamitra pointed out the concealed yakshini to Rama, who drew from his quiver arrows capable of following sound and surrounded her with them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	The powerful female demon, an adept in occult powers, encompassed by the rain of arrows, advanced roaring, towards the princes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	With an arrow, Shri Rama pierced the heart of the wicked yakshini, who fell to the ground and expired.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Seeing the terrible yakshini slain, Indra and other celestial beings worshipped Shri Rama, crying: "Well done, well done, O Holy Rama!"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	All the gods filled with joy, said to Shri Vishvamitra: "O Muni, may prosperity attend you, Indra and the gods are gratified with Shri Ramacandra's feat of arms, show your special favour to him and deliver to him the two kinds of weapons, natural and supernatural, belonging to Krishashva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Present Shri Ramacandra, who is worthy to receive them, with all the other mighty weapons, he is wholly devoted to you; these two princes are destined to achieve great things."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Having uttered these words, the gods bowed down to the Sage Vishvamitra and returned to their abode.
