RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Evening fell, and the holy sage gladdened by the slaying of the wicked Taraka by Shri Rama, smelt the head of the prince and addressed him thus: "O Rama, this night we will remain here and to-morrow morning proceed to my hermitage."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Shri Rama rejoiced to hear the muni's words and rested happily during the night in the forest.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	On the day that Taraka was slain, the forest, freed from the curse, adorned with champaka, ashoka, mango and other trees, looked as charming as the forest of Citraratha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	26_How the Yakshini Taraka was slain	Shri Ramacandra, whom the siddhas praised for slaying Taraka, passed the night in the forest, awaiting the dawn.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	Having passed the night resting in the forest, the illustrious Sage Vishvamitra spoke to Rama smilingly, in sweet accents:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	"O Prince of Great Renown, I am entirely satisfied with you and am happy to give you these weapons by means of which you shalt be able to conquer and subdue all thine enemies, whether devas, asuras or nagas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	Accept these divine weapons, O Rama.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	Here is the great celestial disc and the Dunda weapon, the Disc of Dharma, the Kala weapon, the Disc of Vishnu and the irresistible Weapon of Indra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	O Great Prince, here is the Mace and the Spear of Mahendra the Brahma-Shira and the Ishika.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	O Mighty-armed One, take the Shankara weapon and the two great maces Koumoduki and Lohitamukhi.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	O Great Prince receive also the mighty Dharmapasha, the Kalapasha and the Varunapasha and two other maces called Shoshka and Ashani; the Pinaka weapon, the Narayana weapon and the fire-emitting weapon Agneya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	"O Rama, take this wind weapon, Vayuvya, and the horseheaded weapon, Hayashira, also the Krauncha weapon.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	I give you further two powers and the weapons called Kankala, Mushala, Rapala and Kinkini.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	O Mighty Prince, I confer on you the two supernatural weapons named Vidyadhara and Nandana, useful in fighting the Asuras.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	"Take this jewel among swords, which I give to you, O Mighty-armed One, and another supernatural weapon named Gandharva, and here, O Rama, is one very dear to me called Manava.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	Here are Prashaman, Soura, Prasvaprana, Darpana and that which has the power of drying up, and the paininflicting weapon causing lamentation.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	I grant you also the strength to bear the Madana-astra presented to me by Kandarpa which creates in man unbearable sexual desire so that he is unable to fight.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	Here also is the Paisha-astra and the Mohan-astra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	"O!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	Illustrious Prince, receive also the weapon that produces inertia, and the great Saumana weapon.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	O Great Prince, here are the Samvartta, Moushalya, Sattyastra and Mayadhara, and take the Tajaprabha by means of which the strength and courage of the foe are withdrawn, and also the Shishira which chills and the Somastra and Twashtra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	"O Rama, now you are all-powerful and knowest the secrets of magic, yet take the Bava, Shitesu and Manava astra also.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	O Prince, receive the Paramodara-astra, take all these weapons from me."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	Then the great Vishvamitra turned his face to the east and performed the purificatory rites with joy, conferring on Rama the mantrams for employing the weapons and instructing him in the methods unknown even to the gods.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	AD these weapons did Shri Vishvamitra confer on Rama, and he, repeating the appropriate mantrams, caused their presiding deities to appear before him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	Approaching with joined palms, they said: "O Prince of the House of Raghu, we are your servants and wiD obey your behests."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	Shri Rama, having surveyed and blessed them, answered: "Come and serve me when I summon you."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	27_Shri Rama is given the celestial weapons	Thereafter, Shri Ramacandra offering salutations to the venerable Sage Vishvamitra, said: "Let us proceed further, my Lord."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	Having received the weapons and instructions for their use, Shri Rama addressed the sage in charming accents as they proceeded onward.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	He said: "O Blessed One, by your grace, I have received weapons which even the devas and asuras cannot easily obtain.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	Be pleased to tell me further, how I may withdraw these weapons when they are discharged?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	Then the supremely patient and holy sage taught Shri Ramacandra the method of withdrawing the mantra-propelled weapons and gave him more by the name of Satyavana, Satyakirti, Dhrishta, Raphasa, Pratiharatara, Parangmukha, Avangmukha, Lakshya, Alakshya, Drirnabha and Sunabhuka, Dasharsha, Shutavaktra, Dashashirsha, Shatodara, Dharmanabha and Mahanabha, Dundanabha and Svanabhuka, Jyotisha and Shakuna and the two weapons Nirashya and Vimala, also the Yogandhara and Vinidra, Ditya and Pramanthana, Shuchivahu, Mahavanu, Nishkali, Viruca, Sarchimali Dhriti and Mali, Vrittiman and Rucira, Pitryia and Soamanasvidhuta and Makara, Karavira with Rati, Dhana and Dhanya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	The holy sage said, "O Rama, receive also Kamarupa, Kamaruci, Moha and Avarana, also Jrim Bhala, Sarpanatha with Sandhana and Varuna.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	Receive from me, O Rama, the Krishashva which assumes any form--O Prince, mayest you be triumphant, you are worthy to possess these weapons".
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	Shri Rama answered "May it be so, my Lord".
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	The holy rishi then placed the divine weapons before Rama, some of which shone like fire, others with the colour of smoke and yet others which resembled the sun and moon.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	With joined palms the deities presiding over them addressed Shri Rama with submission, saying: "O Prince, we are at your service, what would'st you have us accomplish?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	Shri Rama answered: "When called to mind in the time of need, grant me aid, now depart, all of you."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	Offering obeisance to Shri Ramacandra, they replied: "Be it so, my Lord," and returned to their abode.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	Shri Rama then questioned the great rishi, saying: "O Spiritual Sovereign, what is this that resembles a dark cloud near the mountain?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	It would seem to be a grove of trees, pleasing to the sight, filled with deer.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	I hear birds singing sweetly, have we then passed the dangerous forest which was a cause of fear?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	O Lord, let us rest here at peace; tell me, whose hermitage is this?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	O Great Muni, are we now in thine own hermitage, where the wicked demons, the slayers of brahmins obstruct your sacrifice?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	O Blessed One, be pleased to show me the place of your sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	O Wise One, I will slay the meddlesome demons who hinder your devotions.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	28_Shri Rama is instructed in their use	Be gracious enough to enlighten me in the matter, O Sage."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	To the most glorious Shri Ramacandra making enquiry concerning the forest, the illustrious Sage Vishvamitra made answer:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	"O Rama, this is the place at which the Blessed Lord Vishnu, the first among the gods, dwelt, observing his yogic practices for immeasurable years and previous to that, it belonged to the glorious Vamana.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	This spot is called Siddha-ashrama, for here, these great souls practised austerities with success.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	At that time, Bali the son of King Virocana, conquered Indra and other devas, together with the deities of the wind and he ruled over the three worlds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	When Bali initiated a sacrifice, the devas, under the leadership of Agni approached Shri Vishnu in this hermitage and said: 'O Lord, the son of Virocana, King Bali is observing a great sacrifice; while it is yet incomplete, come to our aid.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	The Lord grants the requests of those who seek His favour, therefore, by the power of Your Yoga and for our own good, take the form of a dwarf (Vamana) and secure our welfare.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	Meantime, O Rama, the Sage Kashyapa, resplendent as fire, who was endowed with supreme lustre by virtue of his yogic practices, with his spouse Aditi, having completed a thousand years' austerities, began to praise Madhusudana, the conferrer of boons, saying: 'O Supreme Purusha, You are adored through austerity and You dost grant the fruit of austerity, Your nature is knowledge and asceticism, it is by virtue of austerity that I behold You.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	O Lord, in Your body I see the whole world animate and inanimate.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	In You Who art beginningless and indescribable, I take refuge.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	"The blessed Vishnu was pleased with this prayer and said to the sinless Sage: 'O Kashyapa, mayest you see perfection, you have merited a boon, ask what you desirest.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	"Then Kashyapa, the son of Marichi, answered: 'O Blessed Lord, Aditi, the gods and I beseech You to grant this boon--Become the son of my sinless wife and myself.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	O Lord, become the younger brother of Indra and assist the sorrow-stricken devas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	This spot, by Your grace, shall then be known as Siddha-Ashrama.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	(Hermitage of the Perfect Ones.)
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	"Upon this, the resplendent Vishnu was born of the womb of Aditi as the incarnation Vamana and disguised as a mendicant, he approached King Bali.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	Of him, he requested a piece of ground that could be covered by three strides, and having obtained what he asked, he covered the whole universe in three steps.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	"This restful hermitage formerly belonging to Vamana, whose devotee I am, is enjoyed by me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	Here the rakshasas wreak destruction.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	O Lion among men, remain here and slay them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	O Rama, to-day let us enter the Siddha- Ashrama together.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	O Friend, this hermitage is not only mine but thine also."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	Accompanied by Shri Ramacandra and Lakshmana, the holy sage entered the hermitage, which appeared as beautiful as the autumn moon attended by the planet Punarvasu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	When the sages dwelling in the Siddha-Ashrama perceived Shri Vishvamitra, they rose and saluted him with joy.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	Having duly honoured the resplendent sage, they entertained the princes in a fitting manner.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	Having rested awhile, the two princes humbly and respectfully addressed the holy sage, saying: "O Great Sage, inaugurate your sacrifice to-day, may it be attended with good fortune.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	This place is the Siddha-Ashrama, we wish you success in your undertaking."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	Thereupon the great sage with due preparation, his mind subdued, began the sacrifice while the two princes kept vigil.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	29_Vishvamitra relates the story of his hermitage and commences the sacrifice	Having passed the night in this manner, in accordance with the prescribed rules, they performed their ablutions, repeating the mantram silently, they then paid respect to Shri Vishvamitra and occupied their seats as do those performing a fire-sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	The two princes, knowing what was appropriate in respect to time and place and skilled in the art of conquering their foes, uttered words fitting to the place and occasion.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	They said: "O Blessed One, we desire to hear at what moment in the course of the sacrifice, the two demons appear?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	It is essential for us to be acquainted with the matter, to forestall their attack."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	The dwellers in the Siddha-ashrama, hearing the words of the princes, and finding them eager to fight the demons, praised them saying: "O Princes, from now on, keep watch over the sacrifice for six days; the Sage Vishvamitra having begun the rite will observe a strict silence during that time."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	On this, the two illustrious princes kept watch in the Tapovana forest continuously for six days without sleeping.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	Armed with bow and arrows they guarded the rishi and his sacrifice with firm resolve.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	Five days passed without interruption and on the sixth day Shri Ramacandra said to Lakshmana: "Brother, be prepared to-day."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	As Shri Rama uttered these words concerning the approaching conflict with the demons, the altar fire blazed up suddenly.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	The officiating brahmin, the priest and Shri Vishvamitra, who were watching, beheld all the sacrificial implements set on fire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	The sacrifice of the holy sage still proceeding, a great and fearful clamour resounded in the firmament.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	As in the rainy season, clouds cover the sky, so the demons by the power of magic began to course through the air.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	Marica and Suvahu and other demons surrounding the altar, let fall torrents of blood.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	Seeing the altar deluged with blood, Shri Ramacandra and Lakshmana were filled with anger and ran to discover the cause.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	Then they saw Marica and other demons in the sky.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	Raghava beholding the demons rushing towards him, said to Lakshmana, "O Lakshmana, see these evil flesh-eating demons, I shall destroy them with the Manava-weapon, as the wind scatters the clouds
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	So saying, Shri Ramacandra hurled the shining Manava weapon at them and striking the breast of Marica, inflicted a wound.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	Thus smitten, the demon was flung into the sea, a distance of a hundred miles.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	Perceiving Marica reeling, struck senseless by the Manava weapon, Shri Ramacandra addressed Lakshmana, saying: "Behold the power of this great weapon created by the muni 1 Yet, though Marica has been deprived of his senses, he is not dead; verily I shall now destroy those wicked, merciless and sinful blood-drinking demons who obstruct the holy sacrifice."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	So saying, he seized the fireweapon and discharged it at the breast of Suvahu, who straightway fell to the ground and expired.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	On this, Shri Rama destroyed the remaining demons with the air-weapon (Vayuvya).
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	Thus by slaying the obstructors of the sacrifice did Shri Ramacandra bring delight to the hearts of the sages and was worshipped by them as was formerly the victorious Indra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	When the sacrifice had been successfully completed, perceiving the world to be freed from the interference of the asuras, the Rishi Vishvamitra said to Rama:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	30_Maricha and Suvahu obstruct the sacrifice and are slain by Rama	"O Mighty-armed Prince, to-day I have fulfilled my spiritual purpose, you have obeyed the commands of your Guru perfectly, truly you have made the Siddha-Ashrama worthy of its name."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	The great hero, the ever-cheerful Rama, together with Lakshmana having successfully assisted Shri Vishvamitra, passed the night in the hermitage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	At dawn, after purifying themselves, they approached Shri Vishvamitra and offered obeisance to him and the other sages.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	Bowing down before the great muni, who was as resplendent as a blazing fire, they addressed him in submissive tones, saying: "O Great Rishi, we are both your humble servants, what further commands are there for us?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	We are here to obey."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	The other rishis, led by Shri Vishvamitra, listened to the words of Shri Ramacandra and answered saying: "O Great One, the King of Mithila, the righteous Janaka is performing a holy sacrifice and we shall attend it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	O Great Beings, be pleased to accompany us; there you will see a rare and wonderful bow.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	In ancient days this bow was given by the devas to Janaka, it is exceedingly heavy and splendid.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	Neither gandharvas nor asuras can bend this great bow, how much less man?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	To test their skill, great kings have come to the assembly of King Janaka, but none has succeeded in raising the bow and stringing it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	O Illustrious One, let us go and see the sacrifice of the King of Mithila and also that marvellous bow.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	In former days, King Janaka performed a sacrifice and the fruit of it was the great bow which he obtained from the gods who instructed him saying: 'Place this bow in the sacrificial chamber and let it be worshipped with incense, perfume and lights
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	Shri Vishvamitra having related these facts, started out accompanied by the two princes and other sages.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	Invoking the Vanadevata (Forest Deity) he said to him: "My sacrifice has come to a successful conclusion, may happiness be thine.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	I am leaving the Siddha-Ashrama for the banks of the sacred river Gunga on the slopes of the Himalayas, situated in the domain of King Janaka."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	Then the sage reverently circumambulated the hermitage and turned northwards.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	As Shri Vishvamitra entered upon his journey, the sages skilled in the knowledge of the science of Brahman, accompanied him with their chattels placed on hundreds of waggons.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	The birds and beasts of the hermitage also followed them for a long way until the holy muni requested them to turn back.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	The sages and the holy muni reached the banks of the river Shona at sunset and, having bathed and recited their evening prayers, performed the fire sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	Shri Ramacandra and Prince Lakshmana then offered salutations to Shri Vishvamitra and the other rishis, and sat down before them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	Thereafter Shri Rama cheerfully enquired: "O Lord, what country is this, covered with verdant groves?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	Be gracious enough to relate everything concerning it."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	31_Vishvamitra starts out with the two princes to attend King Janaka's sacrifice	The great ascetic of firm vows, was pleased to hear these words and, sitting amidst the sages, he described the country fully to them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	"O Rama, in times of yore, there was a king named Kusha, he was the son of a brahmin, a noted ascetic, faithful to his vows, conversant with dharma and ever revered by the virtuous.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	He wedded a high-born woman of great beauty named Bhidharvi, and begat four sons, each resembling himself.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	Their names were Kushamba, Kushanabha, Umuritarajasa and Basu; these four princes were mighty and active, and desirous of teaching them the duties of a kshatriya, the truthful and righteous King Kusha addressed them as follows:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	"'O My Sons, protect and nourish your subjects, this practice is productive of great merit.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	"In order to carry out the instructions of their sire, these princes founded four cities and named them after themselves.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	The mighty Kushamba called his city Kaushambi, and the righteous Kushanabha founded the city of Mahodaya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	O Rama, Prince Umuritarajasa founded the city named Dharmaranya and the Prince Basu called his city Giribrat, also named Basumati.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	This city was surrounded by five mountain peaks and the river Magadhi or Shona meandering through the mountains resembled a lovely garland.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	O Rama, this stream the Magadhi flows towards the east and irrigates the fruitful fields on either bank.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	"O Prince of Raghu, Kushanabha took in wedlock a nymph named Ghritaci and by her had one hundred beautiful daughters, who on reaching maturity were delightful to look upon.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	One day, clad in lovely dresses, in beauty of form unparalleled they wandered in the garden like lightning amidst the clouds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	Singing, dancing and playing on instruments they seemed to be divine forms which had materialised and descended on the earth, or like the stars in the firmament.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	"Seeing those lovely and virtuous princesses, Vayu the wind god thus addressed them:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	'I entreat you all to be wedded to me; give up your mortal form, I will render you immortal.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	Remember youth is passing and youth among mortals passes even more swiftly; wedded to me, you will be beautiful for ever.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	"The damsels listened to the improper speech of the wind god and replied mockingly:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	'O Deity of the Wind, you knowest all that is passing in the hearts of men, but we know what is passing in your heart.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	Why dost you insult us, O Wind?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	O Vayu, who art renowned for your wisdom, we virgins by the power of our devotion and self-control can effect your downfall, but because the merits of the righteous come to nought when they cause harm to others, we shall preserve our sacred vows inviolate.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	O Stupid One, heaven forfend that we choose husbands for ourselves without first seeking the approval of our honoured sire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	He is as a god to us and our master, and we shall wed the husbands he chooses for us.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	"The wind god was enraged and entering their bodies, twisted and distorted them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	Thus afflicted, the princesses in tears, approached their father for assistance.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	"The king was grieved to see his daughters in this condition and said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	'O speak, what has occurred?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	Who, disregarding justice, has deformed you?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	Tell me all.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	32_Vishvamitra tells of his ancestors and the dynasty of King Kusha	The monarch was deeply moved by this event and his heart became heavy."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	When the hundred princesses were thus questioned by the king their father, they placed their heads at his feet and answered: "The wind god, who pervades all, has entered the evil path and desired us to forsake virtuous conduct.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	We told him we were not free to choose our way of life since our father was still living and that he should consult you if he wished to wed us, but that sinful god, disregarding our request has twisted and deformed our bodies in this manner."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	The great king hearing the complaint of the hundred virgins, said to them: "You have acted nobly by practising forbearance towards the deity.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	It is meet that the generous-minded should exercise forbearance, you have added to the honour of our dynasty.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	Forbearance is the chief ornament of both man and woman, you have achieved something rare; few are capable of such forbearance.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	O Virgins, forbearance is charity, forbearance is truth, forbearance is sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	A man's true glory is forbearance; forbearance is dharma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	The world is established in forbearance."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	Having spoken thus, the princesses were comforted, and the king dismissed them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	Then the monarch, mighty like a god, summoned his ministers and consulted them regarding the alliance of his daughters to suitable families at the proper time and place.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	Now a great muni named Chuli full of glory derived from prolonged celibacy and highly virtuous, was engaged in sacred austerities for the purpose of spiritual liberation.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	At that place, the virgin daughter of the nymph Urmila, named Somada, began to minister to the muni.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	She attended on the great sage for a long time with undeviating faith and devotion and her Guru was pleased with her; he said to her: "I am pleased with you, what desire of thine shall I fulfil?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	Perceiving the muni to be highly pleased, that sweet-voiced nymph acquainted with the art of conversation made answer to him: "O King of Kings, I desire to bear a son, resplendent with divine power, a worshipper of God and devoted to dharma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	I have no husband, nor do I wish to be the wife of any, as I am a brahmacarini, therefore, by virtue of your Yoga, grant me a son produced by the power of your thought."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	The divine Sage Chuli was pleased to hear these words and granted her a son named Brahmadatta, by the power of his mind.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	Brahmadatta became King of Kampila and was as prosperous as Indra in heaven.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	King Kushanabha resolved to give his daughters in marriage to King Brahmadatta.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	Kushanabha requested King Brahmadatta to visit him and joyfully gave him his daughters in marriage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	O Ramaji, King Brahmadatta, who was equal to Indra in glory wedded the princesses one by one by taking their hands in his.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	Through the touch of his hand, the princesses were freed from their deformity and restored to their former beauty.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	When King Kushnabha beheld his daughters released from their disfigurement and restored to their former beauty he was filled with joy.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	Thus did the King Kushnabha give his daughters in marriage to King Brahmadatta and then commanded their preceptors to accompany them to the court of his son-in-law.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	33_King Kushanabha's hundred daughters	Somada was delighted with the union of her son to the damsels and receiving them with great affection, commended the virtuous King Kushanabha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	"O Ramaji, after the wedding of his daughters, the sinless King Kushanabha prepared to perform a sacrifice in order to obtain a son.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	"At the inauguration of the sacrifice, the munificent King Kusha, son of Shri Brahma, said to Kushanabha:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	'O my Son, you will obtain a son like thyself, he should be named Gadhi, he will bring you immortal renown.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	"After some time a son was born to the wise King Kushanabha who was a lover of virtue, and his name was Gadhi.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	This Gadhi, O Rama, was my virtuous father and because I was born in the family of Kusha I was called Kaushika.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	"I had, O Prince, an elder sister named Satyavati, who became the faithful spouse of Richika.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	When her lord died, she ascended to heaven and took the form of the Kaushiki river.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	The river is sacred and beautiful, and its waters confer merit on men.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	To bless the world Satyavati became the river flowing near the Himalayas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	"O Prince, through love of my sister, I dwell on the banks of the Kaushiki river near the Himalayas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	"Established in truth, faithful to her lord, that sister of mine, named Satyavati is to-day the river Kaushiki, great among streams and highly fortunate.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	"O Rama, in order to perform a sacrifice, I went to the Siddha ashrama, I have now accomplished my purpose.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	"O Rama, at your instance, I have told you of my family and origin; the night is far spent in listening to this tale, now rest, so that, refreshed, we may resume our journey to-morrow.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	Peace be with you!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	"The leaves of the trees are motionless, the birds and beasts are silent and darkness covers all.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	How imperceptibly the evening has passed away.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	The sky is brilliant with stars, as if a thousand eyes gazed down on us.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	"The bright moon with its cool beams, slowly rising higher and higher dispels the darkness.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	Nocturnal wanderers and the terrible flesh-eating yakshas prowl about here and there."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	Having uttered these words, the great Sage Vishvamitra became silent.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	The other munis praised him saying: "Well spoken, well spoken, O Sage."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	They said: "The dynasty of Kusha has ever practised righteousness and the kings of this line have been eminent in virtue.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	Of this dynasty, you, O Vishvamitra, art the most illustrious, the fame of this royal line has been enhanced by the beautiful river Kaushiki."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	Thus did the great sages praise the Rishi Vishvamitra, who then withdrew to rest, as the sun sets behind a mountain.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	34_Gadhi is the father of Vishvamitra	Shri Ramacandra and his brother Lakshmana, full of wonder also made obeisance to the holy sage and retired to sleep.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	Having passed the night with the other munis on the banks of the river Shona, Shri Vishvamitra said to Prince Rama at daybreak: "Arise, O Prince, the day has dawned, may prosperity attend you!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	Perform your morning devotions and let us prepare for our journey."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	Shri Rama listened to the instructions of the holy sage, recited his morning prayers and prepared to leave, saying: "O Knower of God, the waters of the holy river Shona appear to be very shallow and rest on a sandy bed, be pleased to instruct us where we should cross over it."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	The sage replied: "O Prince, I will show you where the great rishis traversed it."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	Thereafter they forded the river and journeyed on and on, enjoying the many beautiful woods and forests through which they passed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	After proceeding a great distance, late one afternoon, they reached the holy river Ganges, beloved of the sages.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	On beholding the lovely river rendered beautiful by the presence of swans and cranes, Rama, Lakshmana and the sages were filled with delight.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	They halted on the banks and bathed in the sacred river as prescribed by the holy ordinance, then lighting their sacrificial fires they partook of the remains of the offerings.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	According to the tradition, they offered water to their ancestors and spreading coverings, seated themselves by the holy Ganges.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	Sitting in the midst of the sages with the two princes before him, Shri Vishvamitra was questioned by Shri Rama in the following manner:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	"O Lord, I desire to hear the story of this holy river, which traverses the three paths.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	How does the sacred Gunga, passing through the three worlds merge at last in the ocean?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	On this request, Shri Vishvamitra began to narrate the origin and genesis of the sacred river.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	"O Rama, the great Himavat, Lord of the Himalayas, the treasury of all precious metals, had two daughters, who were unsurpassed in loveliness on earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	Their mother Mena, the wife of Himachala (Himavat) was the daughter of Mount Meru.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	Her elder daughter was named Gunga and the younger Uma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	"The devas wishing to observe certain sacred rites, asked for Shri Gunga to promote the success of their undertaking and with the permission of her father, took her away with them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	"Himachala, mindful of the good of all beings, gave his daughter Gunga, the purifier of the whole world, to the gods, thinking it to be his duty to do so.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	The gods supremely gratified took his daughter Gunga and blessing all, left Himachala.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	"O Prince of the House of Raghu, the other daughter of Himachala, named Uma, practised great asceticism, considering it to be her chief wealth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	Himachala gave this ascetic daughter Uma, who was venerated by the whole world, to Shri Mahadeva in marriage, thinking him to be a worthy consort.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	"O Rama, now I have told you of the two daughters of Himachala, revered by the whole world, the river Gunga and Uma Devi.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	"O my Son, O Chief of Disciples, I have related to you the story of Shri Gunga accompanying the devas to heaven.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	35_Vishvamitra begins to narrate the origin of the holy river Ganga	This beautiful daughter of the King of Himalaya, once resident in heaven, is the charming river Gunga, whose waters destroy all sin."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	Hearing the wonderful narrative, so eloquently related by Shri Vishvamitra, both the princes praised the holy sage and said: "O Divine Sage, you have told us a tale, by the hearing of which great merit is acquired, be gracious enough to enlighten us further regarding the elder daughter of the King of Himalaya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	You are omniscient, therefore describe to us fully, how the Gunga, the world purifying stream, came down from heaven to earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	O You, versed in the science of dharma, why is this sacred river called Tripathaga (the Traverser of the Three Worlds) and whence is this name derived?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	Seated amidst the other sages, Shri Vishvamitra, whose only wealth was truth and austerity, spoke as follows, in answer to Shri Rama's questioning:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	"O Prince, in ancient times, the holy Lord Mahadeva was wedded to Parvati and being charmed with her beauty devoted himself to the delights of connubial bliss.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	According to the measure of time of the gods, the Lord Mahadeva passed a hundred years with that devi but remained without issue.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	In their anxiety, the gods approached Shri Brahma and said:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	"'Who will be able to endure the power and glory of the offspring produced by these two mighty beings?'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	"They then took refuge with Shri Mahadeva, saying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	'O God of Gods, O Mahadeva, ever engaged in doing good to all beings, we offer salutations to you, be gracious unto us!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	Your power, O First among the Gods, none can endure, therefore with this goddess engage in yogic penances.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	For the welfare of the three worlds, retain thine energy within your body so that the universe may be preserved and may not suffer destruction'."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	The Ruler of the World, Shri Mahadeva, listened to the words of the devas and said: "Be it so, O Devas, I will restrain my power so that all the regions including the earth may dwell in peace, but O Devas, should my vital fluid overflow, who shall receive it?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	The gods answered Shri Mahadeva, saying: "Let the earth receive it."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	Then Shri Mahadeva let fall his seed on the earth covering the mountains, seas and forests.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	When the earth could bear no more, the devas asked the wind and fire deities to combine with that creative power and thus was a white mountain created and later a heavenly forest as resplendent as the light of the sun.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	From this fiery light was born the glorious Swami Karttikeya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	"All the gods and rishis were full of joy and adored the Lord Shiva and the goddess Uma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	As they worshipped them with grateful hearts, Uma was filled with wrath and said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	'O Devas, your action has filled me with displeasure, you shall not escape the consequences.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	"Then Uma shining like the sun, took water in the palm of her hand and pronounced a curse on the gods, saying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	'O Devas, you have prevented me from bearing a son, may you be childless from this day, may your wives be without progeny.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	"Still not appeased, Uma cursed the earth also and said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	'O Earth, you shalt never remain in one form, you shalt have many masters.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	O Witless One, you shalt never bear a son, since you have prevented me from becoming a mother.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	"Shri Mahadeva, seeing the devas discomfited, prepared to depart to the northern region of the Himalayas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	There, on a peak named Himavatprabhava, he engaged in prolonged yogic practices together with Uma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	36_The story of the king of Himalayas' younger daughter Uma	"O Rama, I have told you of one of the two daughters of the Himalayas; now with Lakshmana, listen to the tale of the other daughter of Himalaya, named Gunga."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	Whilst Shri Mahadeva was engaged in yogic meditation, the devas, under the leadership of Agni, went to the region of Brahma where, with Indra, they paid reverence to the Lord of the world, and said: "O Lord, at the beginning of creation you did'st make Shri Mahadeva our leader, but he has now retired to the Himalayas and is engaged in the practice of austerity with Uma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	O You who art desirous of the good of the world, do what you considerest ought to be done, you are our only refuge."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	Then Shri Brahma encouraged the devas, with gentle words, saying: "O Devas, the curse of Uma Devi, that you should remain without offspring is irrevocable, but the fire god Agni will cause Ganga to bear a son who will destroy the enemies of the gods.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	The youngest daughter of Himancala (Uma) will look upon her sister's son as her own and will inevitably lavish her affection on him."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	"O Rama, the words of Shri Brahma filled the gods with satisfaction and they offered obeisance to him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	Then they all circumambulated Mount Kailasha, the repository of precious metals, and begged Agni to beget a son.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	"Agni acquiesced in their request and approaching Shri Ganga, said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	'O Devi, let us beget a son for it is the wish of the gods.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	"Assuming the form of a celestial nymph, Ganga, inspired the fire god to plant his seed in her, her every vein being filled with splendour.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	After a time, she addressed Agni, saying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	'O Deva, I am unable to bear the ever-increasing splendour which you have communicated to me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	My body is burning like fire, my mind is agitated and I am filled with fear.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	"Agni replied:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	'O Sinless One, place this foetus near the Himalayas.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	"Then Ganga Devi expelled the resplendent being, shining like gold.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	This substance, falling on the earth, became the purest gold that can be found.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	All objects in its proximity became silver and the more distant areas exposed to its penetrating rays became copper, the baser parts becoming zinc and lead.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	In this way, its brilliance was transmuted into metals and spread abroad and the mountains and forests near by were changed to gold.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	O Rama, gold being produced in that dazzling form is called jatarupa (form-bom) and, O Hero, that is why gold shines like fire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	The grass, the creepers, the shrubs, all were converted into gold, and from that splendour was born Kumara.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	"The devas with Indra engaged the Krittikas to nurse the child and they regarded him as their own son.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	The gods named the child Karttikeya and said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	'He shall be our son and he will be renowned in the three worlds.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	"The Krittikas bathed the child and as he grew, his form resembled the fire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	Because the infant was born prematurely, the devas called him Skanda.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	"The nurses began to nourish the child with milk and he shone like a flame.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	With six mouths he sucked the milk of six nurses at the same time.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	Soon he grew so powerful that while yet an infant he challenged groups of demons to combat.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	Then all the gods appointed him their commander-in-chief.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	The Devas and Agni paid affectionate homage to this child.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	"O Rama, this is the inspiring and merit-bestowing story of Shri Ganga and Karttikeya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	37_The king's elder daughter, Ganga	"O Raghava, on this earth, those who read this narrative with faith and devotion shall have long lives, sons and grandsons and obtain the divine region of Skanda."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	Shri Vishvamitra in gentle accents, related this story to Shri Ramacandra, and then again addressed him, saying:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"In ancient times there lived a king named Sagara, who ruled in Ayodhya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	He was brave and virtuous and a lover of his subjects, yet he was without issue.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"The name of his chief queen was Keshini, a daughter of King Vidharba; she was virtuous and truthful.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	His second queen was Sumati, a daughter of Arishtanemi and she was comely and charming.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"The king went to the Himalayas and engaged in severe yogic practices in the forest of Bhriguprasravana.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	When he had completed a hundred years' ascetic practices, the ever truthful Maharishi Bhrigu was pleased with hifn and favoured him with a boon.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	He said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	'O Sinless King, you shalt beget many sons and your fame will be immeasurable.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	From one of your queens shall be born one son, and from the other sixty thousand sons.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"When the queens heard of the boon granted by the rishi, they approached him saying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	'O Knower of God, we are certain that your boon will bear fruit, please tell us therefore which of us will beget one son and which sixty thousand?'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"Hearing their words, the highly virtuous Bhrigu said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	'That depends on your desires.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	Tell me, which of you would fain be the mother of the founder of the dynasty and which desires to beget sixty thousand illustrious sons?'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"O Rama, Queen Keshini desired to be favoured by one son only, but Sumati, the sister of Garuda obtained the boon of bearing sixty thousand powerful and illustrious sons.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"O Prince, the king offered salutations to the Rishi Bhrigu and with his consorts returned to the capital.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"When the time was ripe, the chief Queen Keshini gave birth to a son who was called Asamanjasa.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"O Great One, a gourd was brought forth by Queen Sumati from which, when opened, sixty thousand male infants emerged.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	The nurses placed them in jars full of butter and tended them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	After a long time they attained to the state of adolescence, and then grew to manhood.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"O Rama, the eldest son of King Sagara, Asamanjasa used to seize hold of children and throw them into the river Sarayu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	When he saw them drowning, he rejoiced.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	This evil doer grew up to oppress the good by his conduct.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"The citizens of King Sagara's capital exiled the prince, thus passing judgment on him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	Asamanjasa became the father of a valiant prince named Amshuman, who was esteemed by everyone and addressed every man with courtesy.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	"After a long time, King Sagara resolved to perform a sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	38_The story of King Sagara, Shri Rama's ancestor	O Rama, the king summoning the high priests began the initiatory rites."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	Having listened to this tale, Shri Rama addressed the Muni Vishvamitra, who resembled the fire in splendour, and said: "O Wise One, may prosperity constantly attend you!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	I desire to hear how my ancestor King Sagara performed the sacrifice."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	Shri Vishvamitra, highly gratified by Shri Rama's eager enquiry, smilingly replied: "Listen, O Rama, to the history of the high-souled King Sagara.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	There is a country between the Himalayas and the Vindhya mountains, and it was there that King Sagara performed his sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	That land is suitable for this purpose, O Great Prince.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	"The great archer and warrior Amshuman was appointed the protector of the horse released for the sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	A rakshasa in disguise, stole the horse and when it was being borne away, the priests approached the king, crying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	'See, someone is carrying off the horse, kill the thief and restore it.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	The king called for his sixty thousand sons and said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	'A wicked demon has stolen the sacrificial steed, in what direction has he borne it away?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	It has been consecrated by mantrams to avoid obstructions; seek the horse, my sons, and may success attend you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	Scour the earth surrounded by the seas, and excavate the earth at my command, till the sacred horse is found.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	Having taken the initiation, I cannot leave this place.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	Go You, My Sons I I shall remain here with Amshuman and the brahmins.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	"O Rama, commanded by their father, those powerful princes joyfully started in search of the horse.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	O Great One 1 they ranged the world in vain and began to dig the ground with their nails which were as sharp as diamonds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	"O Prince of the House of Raghu, they used ploughs, spades and other implements to excavate the ground and the earth shook with the sound.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	While ploughing up the earth, many snakes, demons and powerful titans were slain and injured.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	"O Raghava, those mighty princes pierced the earth to the depth of sixty thousand miles and reached the antipodes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	Having pierced the earth with its mountains, they searched for the horse in Jambudvipa.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	"The devas, gandharvas, asuras and nagas became agitated, and approached Shri Brahma; bowing before him with their minds afflicted and in great distress, they said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	'O Blessed Lord, the sons of the Maharajah Sagara are digging up the whole earth and they have brought about the death of many great beings.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	39_The horse with which Sagara performs a sacrifice is stolen	Whosoever opposes them is slain with the words, "You are a thief, you have stolen the sacrificial horse"'."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"The grandsire Shri Brahma, hearing the words of the gods regarding the sons of King Sagara, who were already doomed, said:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"'O Devas, this whole world belongs to the glorious Vasudeva and he, in the form of the Sage Kapila, supports it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	These princes will fall victims to the wrath of holy Kapila; the earth is eternal and cannot be destroyed.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	The gods, hearing these words, returned to their own regions, full of joy.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"Meanwhile, the uproar caused by the sons of Sagara digging the earth resembled the crash of thunder.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"Having encompassed the whole world, they returned to their father and said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	'We have traversed the whole world and have slain gods, demons and snakes, but we have found no trace of the sacrificial horse nor of the thief.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	O Father, may prosperity attend you, be pleased to reflect on the matter and give us further instructions.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"The great monarch replied in anger:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	'Go, dig the earth once more, capture the horse, accomplish your purpose, then return.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"In accordance with the command of their royal sire, the princes once more renewed their tunnelling and came upon the monstrous form of a great elephant which resembled a mountain.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"O Prince of Raghu, the whole earth and the mountains of that quarter are supported by that elephant Vimpaksha, and whenever, from fatigue, he moves his feet to ease himself, the whole world trembles and quakes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"The princes bowed down to him and circumambulated him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	They then continued digging deeper and deeper, first to the east, then to the west.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	To the south they saw the second great elephant whose name was Mahapadma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	They beheld him supporting that quarter of the earth and were astonished; they offered him salutations.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"O Prince, the sons of King Sagara next dug the northern quarter of the earth and saw there a white elephant which resembled a heap of snow.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	His name was Hima-Pandara and his form was gigantic; they worshipped him as he stood supporting that quarter of the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"Then with furious zeal, those mighty and valiant sons of Sagara dug the earth and proceeded to that renowned quarter where they saw Kapila the eternal Lord Vasudeva and the horse grazing near him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"O Rama, they were glad, thinking that it was Shri Kapila who had stolen the horse.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	Full of wrath, seizing ploughs, trees, rocks and stones, they ran towards him, crying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	'You are the stealer of the sacrificial horse, you are the thief.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	O Wicked One, we, the sons of King Sagara, have found you.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	40_The king's sons search for the horse; they accuse Shri Kapila of stealing it and are reduced to ashes	"O Rama, Shri Kapila, hearing these words, filled with rage, uttered the sound 'H'm' and instantly by his immeasurable power all the sons of Sagara were reduced to ashes."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	"O Ramacandra, perceiving that a long period had elapsed since the departure of his sons, King Sagara spoke to his powerful and resplendent grandson Amshuman:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	"'O Child, you are valiant, learned and illustrious like thine ancestors, go and seek thine uncles and the stealer of the horse also.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	The interior of the earth is inhabited by the most mighty beings, arm thyself therefore with sword, bow and arrows.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	Pay reverence to those worthy to be worshipped whom you dost encounter on the way and make obeisance to them; slay those who obstruct your purpose, then successful, return and ensure the completion of the sacrifice.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	"Thus instructed by his grandfather, Prince Amshuman, arming himself with sword, bow and arrows, speedily departed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	Honoured on the way by devas, danavas, asuras and nagas, pisachas, birds and serpents, he came to the mighty and resplendent elephant and worshipped him, enquiring as to his welfare.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	The elephant said in reply:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	'O Prince Amshuman, you will accomplish your purpose and soon return to the capital.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	"The prince proceeded further and enquired in the same manner of each of the other great elephants.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	They all advised the prince, who had paid due respect to them, to proceed further.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	As instructed by them, Amshuman came to the place where the heaped ashes of his uncles' bodies were lying.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	Overcome with grief, Amshuman wept to see that death had overtaken them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	Afflicted with distress and pain, he suddenly perceived the sacrificial horse grazing near by.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	Desirous of offering the rite of water for his departed relatives, he looked round but could find no water anywhere.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	Extending his gaze, he saw his maternal uncle, the holy eagle, who addressed the prince as follows:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	"'O Lion among men, grieve not, these princes have met the death they deserved.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	They have been consumed to ashes by the Mahatma Kapila of unimaginable glory.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	O Wise One, it is not meet to offer the usual rites for them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	O Great One, perform the rites with the water of the holy river Ganga, the Daughter of Himalaya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	When the waters of the purifier of the world, the sacred Ganga flow over their ashes, the ceremony will be crowned with success and the sixty thousand princes will be received into heaven'."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	The illustrious and mighty Prince Amshuman listened to the words of Shri Garuda and speedily returning with the horse, approached King Sagara, who still awaited the completion of the initiatory rites; he related to him all that the eagle had said.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	The monarch completed the sacrifice and returned to his capital considering the means whereby he might cause Shri Ganga to descend to earth; but in vain.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	41_King Sagara's grandson, Amshuman, finds the horse and the ashes of his uncles	King Sagara, unable to devise any way to accomplish this matter, having ruled for thirty thousand years, departed hence.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	After his death, the ministers installed the virtuous Amshuman as king.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	O Rama, glorious was the reign of King Amshuman.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	He was succeeded by his son, the world-renowned Dilipa.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	King Amshuman, leaving his kingdom to Dilipa, retired to the top of a Himalayan peak and began to perform severe yogic austerities.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	Having passed thirty-two thousand years in this wise, without inducing the sacred river Ganga to descend on earth, he gave up his life.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	Acquainted with the fate of his great uncles, and overcome with grief, the mighty sovereign Dilipa found no means of bringing the sacred stream down to earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	Consumed with anxiety, he reflected daily on how he should accomplish the descent of the Ganga and perform the funeral rites for the deliverance of the souls of his ancestors.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	The righteous and illustrious King Dilipa, constantly engaged in these reflections, was then blessed with the birth of a virtuous son, Bhagiratha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	The renowned monarch Dilipa observing many sacrifices, ruled over his kingdom for thirty thousand years; his thoughts were ever devoted to the deliverance of the souls of his forbears until stricken with disease, he was claimed by death.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	Having bequeathed the kingdom to his son Bhagiratha, his spirit ascended to the region of Indra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	O Rama, Bhagiratha was a virtuous and royal sage, but he had no heir and was desirous of obtaining a son.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	O Raghava, he entrusted the administration of his kingdom to his ministers and proceeded to the holy place named Gokama where he practised yogic penances to attract the descent of the holy Ganga.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	With arms uplifted and senses controlled, he stood in the midst of five fires in the hottest season, partaking of food once a month only, and continued thus for a thousand years.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	O Mighty Prince, after a thousand years, Shri Brahma, the Lord and Ruler of the world, was pleased with Bhagiratha and, accompanied by the devas, approached the high-souled king and said:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	"O Bhagiratha, your virtuous yogic practices have elicited our admiration; ask for a boon, O Fortunate One."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	The highly resplendent Bhagiratha, with joined palms submissively addressed Shri Brahma, saying: "O Blessed Lord, if you are pleased to confer the fruits of mine austerities on me and grant me a boon, then allow me to deliver the souls of the sons of King Sagara by offering them water at their funeral rites, from the sacred stream.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	O Lord, do you also grant as a further boon that the Dynasty of Ikshvaku may be preserved and I may have an heir."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	The Grandsire of the whole world listened to the prayer of the Maharajah Bhagiratha and answered him in gentle and pleasing accents:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	"O Mighty King Bhagiratha, you have asked a great boon, may success attend you!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	Let your desire for a son be fulfilled.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	O King, when the Ganga, the eldest daughter of Himalaya falls on the earth with overwhelming power, the earth will not be able to sustain her; none but the Lord Shiva can accomplish this."
