RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	42_Bhagiratha performs austerities to induce the holy river to descend	Having uttered these words to King Bhagiratha and having spoken to Shri Ganga also, Shri Brahma returned with the gods to his own region.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Shri Brahma having departed, the King Bhagiratha, standing on the tip of one toe, adored Shri Shiva for a full year.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	O Mighty One, with arms uplifted, living on air, unsupported, fixed like a pillar, day and night King Bhagiratha offered his adorations to the Lord.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	A full year having passed, the Lord of Uma, Shri Mahadeva, who is adored by the whole world, spoke to King Bhagiratha as follows: "O Great One, I am pleased with you, I will accomplish what you desirest, I will receive the descent of Ganga on my head."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Then the holy Ganga, the eldest daughter of Himalaya, the object of reverence to the whole world, assuming the form of a mighty river, descended with torrential force on to the head of Shiva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	The goddess reflected within herself that she would bear down the Lord Mahadeva to the antipodes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Shri Shiva, reading her thoughts, grew angry and determined to detain the mighty stream in his hair.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Resembling the majestic Himalayas, the locks of Shri Shiva held the falling Ganga fast and the sacred river remained imprisoned there.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	For innumerable years the Ganga wandered round and round in the locks of Shri Mahadeva and could not find an egress.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	O Rama, when Shri Bhagiratha did not see the holy stream descending to earth, he again began his penance in order to propitiate the Lord of the world.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Then Shri Shiva let loose the Ganga in the Brindusara lake and as it fell it divided itself into seven streams.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	The three branches conferring prosperity, Hladini, Pavani and Nalini, flowed towards the east from the head of holy Shiva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Then the sacred Ganga of pure and delightful water was divided into three further branches, Sucakshu, Sita and Sindhav, all flowing towards the west.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	The seventh of these streams followed the chariot of the Maharajah Bhagiratha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	The royal sage, riding in a beautiful chariot, went forward and the sacred river Ganga followed him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Thus did the holy river descend from heaven on to the forehead of Shri Mahadeva and from thence came to the surface of the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	The fall of the sacred stream created a mighty reverberation, her waters flowing through beautiful ways.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Riding their aerial chariots as large as cities, containing elephants and horses, the gods, sages, celestial musicians, yakshas and siddhas in great numbers, came to witness the holy Ganges falling from heaven to earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	In their aerial chariots named Pariplava, the gods came to see this wonderful event of the holy river flowing on the earth, and as they descended from the skies, the splendour of their celestial ornaments irradiated the cloudless canopy of heaven as if a thousand suns had risen there.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	The mercurial fishes and aquatic creatures leaping from the stream thrown up by the force of the current, shone like lightning in the sky, whilst the foam and spray scattered on all sides resembled flocks of swans in flight or clouds in winter.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	The waters of the holy Ganga sometimes rose high in the air, sometimes flowed tortuously, sometimes broadened out, sometimes dashed against the rocks and sometimes spouted upwards afterwards falling to the ground; that pure water capable of removing sin looked delightful flowing on the surface of the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Then the celestial sages and heavenly musicians and the denizens of the earth, reverently touched that sacred stream falling from the locks of Shiva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Those beings, who through a curse, had fallen from the heavenly regions and been made to dwell on earth, were cleansed of their transgressions by bathing in the holy Ganga.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Purified and freed from their sins, those resplendent beings returned to the heavenly regions, passing through the sky.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Wherever the sacred Ganges flowed, people were cleansed of their sins by bathing in its waters.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	King Bhagiratha, riding a celestial chariot, drove on and Shri Ganga followed after him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	O Rama, the gods, the sages, rakshasas, asuras, yakshas, the chief serpents and nymphs following King Bhagiratha, together with the aquatic beings and swans, attended the sacred river.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Whichever course King Bhagiratha took, that mighty river Ganga, the Destroyer of all sin, followed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Flowing on and on, Shri Ganga arrived where the Sage Jahnu, worker of miracles, was performing a sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Then the sacred river swept over the sacrificial pavilion and all it contained.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	The Rishi Jahnu perceiving the pride of Gangaji, grew angry and drank up the whole of the water of that river, verily a great miracle!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	The devas, gandharvas and sages were astonished and began to worship that Mahatma Jahnu, saying, "From to-day the holy river shall be called your daughter The mighty Jahnu being pleased, let loose the river through his ears.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	From thence Shri Ganga is called Jahnavi (the daughter of Jahnu).
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Thereafter she once again flowed behind the chariot of King Bhagiratha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	Finally, the holy Ganga reached the sea and entered the lower regions to fulfil the purpose of the king.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	The royal Sage Bhagiratha attended by the sacred river, gazed with grief on the ashes of his ancestors.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	43_ Lord Shiva lets loose the sacred river which follows King Bhagiratha's celestial chariot	O Prince of the House of Raghu, as soon as the holy stream touched the ashes, the sons of King Sagara were resuscitated, freed from sin, and attained the celestial region.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	When the king attended by the holy Ganga, reached the seashore, he entered the subterranean region where the sons of King Sagara had been burnt to ashes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	"O Rama, as the holy water flowed over the ashes, Shri Brahma the Lord of all the worlds, addressed King Bhagiratha as follows:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	'O Great King, you have redeemed the sixty thousand sons of King Sagara, who now dwell in the heavenly region.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	O King, as long as the waters of the sea continue on earth, so long shall the sons of King Sagara in celestial form enjoy heaven.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	Henceforth, O Great Sovereign, Shri Ganga shall be your eldest daughter and be known by your name throughout the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	This sacred river shall be named Shri Ganga, Tripathaga and Bhagirathi.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	"'O King, perform the funeral rites of thine ancestors and fulfil your prescribed duty.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	The mighty King Sagara was not able to accomplish this purpose and King Amshuman of limitless prowess also failed to obtain the fulfilment of his devout desire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	Your father Dilipa, equal to ourselves in merit and a warrior fully established in the duties of his caste, that illustrious Dilipa besought the holy Ganga to descend to earth in vain.

RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	"'By achieving this, you are possessed of the highest dharma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	O Great Sovereign, now do you bathe in the holy stream also.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	O Lion among men, purify thyself and acquire merit, then perform the funeral rites of thine ancestors.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	O King, may prosperity attend you, return to your capital, I shall now ascend to my own abode.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	"The mighty and illustrious Brahma then ascended to heaven and the royal Sage Bhagiratha, having performed the obsequies of the sons of King Sagara, with the water of the sacred Ganges, returned to his capital.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	"Enjoying every felicity, King Bhagiratha began to govern once more and his people rejoiced that he had again assumed rulership.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	All were freed from suffering and anxiety and they increased in wealth and prosperity.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	"O Rama, I have narrated the story of the descent of Shri Ganga fully to you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	May prosperity attend you I Dusk has fallen and the hour of the evening prayer has come.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	This story gives wealth, prosperity, fame, longevity, sons, and residence in heaven to the reader.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	He who causes it to be heard by others whether he be a brahmin or a kshatriya, brings joy to his ancestors and the gods.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	44_King Bhagiratha completes the funeral rites for his ancestors	"O Ramacandra, he who with fixed attention listens to this story, shall obtain all he desires, his sins will be remitted and he will obtain long life and renown."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Shri Ramacandra and Shri Lakshmana were filled with astonishment on hearing the words of Shri Vishvamitra, and said to him: "O Holy Sage, marvellous indeed is the history of King Sagara and the descent of the Ganges, which you have related to us."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	The night drew on as they had been listening to the story, and Shri Rama and Lakshmana passed the remaining hours meditating on the matter.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	The clear day dawned and Shri Rama, having performed his daily devotions, said to Shri Vishvamitra: "The night has passed in listening to this divine narrative, it has slipped away, as if it were a moment.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Now let us cross the sacred and merit-giving stream reflecting on its marvellous origin.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Knowing you to have come, the other sages have sent a boat in preparation for crossing the holy river."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Shri Vishvamitra summoned the ferryman and with the princes and sages all were conveyed to the other side.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	They rested awhile on the opposite bank and entertained the sages in their company.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	In the distance, they saw the city named Vishala and soon the great Rishi Vishvamitra with the princes reached that place of beauty, which resembled one of Indra's cities.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Then Rama, full of wisdom, approached the holy sage and humbly made enquiry concerning the city.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	He said: "O Great Sage, what royal and illustrious house rules here?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	I desire to hear."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	At these words of Rama, the holy sage began to relate the story of the city as follows:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"O Rama, attend!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	I will tell you the story of this city, which I heard from Indra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"In the golden age (Satya Yuga) Diti gave birth to a powerful son Daitya, an asura, and Aditi gave birth to the highly fortunate and exceedingly righteous son Devata, a celestial being.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	These two sagacious beings sought to become immortal, incorruptible and free from disease, old age and other ills.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	After reflecting on this matter, they resolved to chum Kshiroda (the ocean of milk) and obtain from it the water of immortality.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Using the mighty snake Vasuki as a rope and the Mandara mountain as the churn, they began to churn the ocean.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	When they had done so for a thousand years, the snake Vasuki bit the rocks with its teeth and threw up venom.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	From this was produced the great poison which began to consume men, gods, demons and the whole world.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"The gods took refuge with the Lord Shiva and worshipped him crying 'Protect us, protect us'.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Attracted by the mournful cry of the gods, Shri Mahadeva and Shri Hari appeared there with conch and disc.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"Shri Vishnu smilingly addressed the bearer of the trident, Shri Mahadeva, and said: 'O Lord, you are the chief of the gods and should'st, therefore, accept whatever is first produced by the churning of the ocean.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Receive the poison as your gift, the first tribute.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"Having spoken thus, Shri Vishnu disappeared, and the Blessed Lord Shiva, moved by the distress of the gods and the words of Shri Vishnu, drank the dreadful poison, as if it were nectar, and returned to Kailasha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"O Prince of Raghu, the devas and the daityas began churning once more, but the churning staff began to sink.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Then the devas and gandharvas praised the Lord Vishnu, saying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	'O Blessed Lord, You are the Master of all beings, you are the asylum of the gods--protect us all, O Great Lord, and support the sinking Mandara mountain'.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"Shri Vishnu, assuming the form of a tortoise, entered the ocean and supported the mountain on his back.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Taking hold of the peak in his hand, the blessed Vishnu churned the ocean, standing between the devas and the asuras.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"After a thousand years, Shri Dhanvantari, the teacher of the Ayur Veda appeared, holding a staff and loshta in his hands; thereafter many nymphs emerged.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	O Raghava, they were called apsaras, 'ap' meaning water and 'yara' to 'emerge from'; on this account these beautiful damsels were named 'apsaras'.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	O Rama, they numbered six hundred million and their female attendants were innumerable.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	None were received either by the devas or the daityas, hence they remained without a lord.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"Then, O Prince, Varuni, the daughter of the god Varuna was born.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	The sons of Aditi did not accept her, but the asuras gladly did so.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Those who rejected her were called suras (devas) and those who received her became merry and were called asuras.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"O Raghava, then the celestial horse Uccaihshravas and the jewel Kaustubha also rose out of the sea, and they were succeeded by the water of immortality.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"O Rama, the devas fought with the danavas for possession of the nectar and the daityas allied themselves with the asuras in this struggle; terrible indeed was this combat.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"After many had lost their lives in the fight, Shri Vishnu assumed the form of Mohini, a charming woman the product of Maya and stole the nectar from the combatants.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	"Those who opposed the imperishable Vishnu were destroyed by him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	In this conflict the gods slew countless daityas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	45_The city of Vishala and the churning of the ocean	Indra, after slaying the asuras, became the king of the devas and with the help of the sages began to rule with joy."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	"O Rama, learning that her children had been slain, Diti was much afflicted and approached her husband Kasyapa with the words:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	''O Lord, by your powerful sons, am I bereft of my children.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	I desire a son who will be able to destroy Indra, though to this end I must undergo great penance.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	Such austerities I will perform, if you will grant me a son that is mighty, valorous, strong-willed and firm of purpose.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	'"The holy sage answered the afflicted Diti saying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	''Be it so!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	Remain chaste for a thousand years, you shalt then bear a son capable of destroying Indra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	By my grace, your child shall be the ruler of the three worlds.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	'"Thus did the sage console Diti, and blessing her, departed to practise penance.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	Diti retired contentedly to the forest of Kushaplava and began to undergo severe austerities.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	'"Indra then, coming there, paid reverence to her and began to serve her with humility, supplying her with fire, kusha grass and other necessities, massaging her body when she became weak from the severity of ascetic practices.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	O Rama, Indra served Diti for a thousand years less ten days.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	'"Then Diti joyfully addressed Indra saying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	''O Indra, your father has promised to grant me a son after a thousand years penance.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	You shalt soon behold your brother, whom I desire shall overcome you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	With him you shalt share the three worlds and be happy, have no anxiety.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	'"By this time the afternoon had come.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	Diti overcome with sleep, placing her feet where her head had lain, carelessly assumed an impure posture.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	'"Indra rejoiced and laughed aloud.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	Entering her body, he cut the foetus into seven pieces with his great mace.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	Diti's slumber was interrupted by the cry of the child in her womb.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	'Indra said to it 'Do not weep', 'Do not weep', and again divided the child with his mace, despite Diti's cries, 'Do not destroy it, do not destroy it'.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	'"Then Indra paused in his murderous assault and with extreme humility addressed Diti saying
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	''O Did, you wast impure through sleeping with your feet towards the head of the couch, you did'st thus occupy an improper posture.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	I have, therefore, severed thine unborn child into seven parts, since he was to be the cause of my destruction.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	46_Diti undergoes severe austerities for the birth of a son	O Devi, pardon me'."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	Knowing the foetus to be divided into seven parts, Diti was greatly perturbed and said to Indra:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	"Through my fault has this come to pass; O Indra, you are in no wise guilty.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	This child being divided, for your good and mine own, I declare that these seven shall become the protectors of the forty-nine winds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	These seven sons of divine appearance shall be known as the Bala-kanda winds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	Let one wander about in the region of Brahma, another in the region of Indra, and the third in space.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	Let the remaining four winds go anywhere under your instructions; may they all be known by the name of Maruts, conferred on them by you."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	With joined palms, the thousand-eyed god Indra said in reply to Diti: "O Devi, it will assuredly come to pass as you desires.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	Your sons shall wander about in the form of devas in the Tapovana forest."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	Thus reconciled and fully satisfied the mother and son ascended to heaven.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	Thus have I heard, O Rama!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	This is that Tapovana forest in which Indra formerly served his mother Diti.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	O Lion among Men, here a great city was founded by the righteous Prince Vishala, the son of King Ikswaku and Alambusa.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	O Rama, the mighty son of Vishala was named Hemacandra, and his son was the renowned Sucandra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	O Rama, the son of Sucandra was Dhumrashva and his son was Srinjaya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	The glorious Sahadeva was the son of Srinjaya and the son of Sahadeva was the highly virtuous Krishashva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	The son of Krishashva was Somadatta and his son was Kakustha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	The most illustrious and invincible of warriors King Pramati the son of Kakustha, is the present ruler of Vishala.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	By the grace of King Ikswaku all the rulers of Vishala are long lived, virtuous and mighty.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	O Rama, let us pass the night here, and to-morrow we will wait upon King Janaka.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	When the powerful King Pramati heard of Shri Vishvamitra's arrival in his kingdom, he went with his spiritual preceptor and relatives to welcome him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	With joined palms, they offered him due worship and enquired as to his welfare.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	The king said: "O Muni, to-day I am indeed fortunate that you have been gracious enough to visit my kingdom.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	47_The holy sage and the princes arrive at Vishala and are welcomed by King Pramati	None is more blessed than I."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	King Pramati having enquired as to the well-being of Shri Vishvamitra, said:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	"O Holy Sage, may the Lord protect those two youths; be gracious enough to tell me who they may be.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	These princes, equal to the gods in power, walking with the gait of an elephant, fearless as lions or bulls in combat, whose eyes resemble lotuses, who are armed with swords, bows and quivers, who rival the heavenly Asvins in beauty and who, in the flower of their youth, appear like gods, visiting the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Why are they travelling on foot?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Whose sons are they?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Why are they come?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Enhancing the earth as the sun and moon illumine the sky; their manner of address and bearing showing them to be kinsmen, why are these two heroes of high descent, bearing mighty weapons, found on this hard path?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	I long to hear."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Shri Vishvamitra related to the king the whole story of the visit to the Siddha Ashrama and the slaying of the asuras.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	The king was highly gratified to meet the princes, and perceiving them to be virtuous, entertained them with the greatest respect.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Shri Ramacandra and Lakshmana having received hospitality from King Pramati, passed the night there.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	The following day they left for Mithilapuri, the capital of King Janaka.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	When they beheld the city at a distance, they cried out: "How beautiful, how beautiful it is!"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Thereafter, finding a charming hermitage which was uninhabited, Rama enquired of the Rishi Vishvamitra as follows: "O Sage, how can it be that this beautiful hermitage is unfrequented?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	O Lord, tell us whose has been this hermitage?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Shri Vishvamitra, chief among the eloquent, answered Rama, saying: "O Prince, hear the true story of this hermitage, I will relate to you who was its author and how he cursed it in anger.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	"O Rama, this place, a source of wonder even to the gods, belonged to the Rishi Gautama and resembled the abode of the celestials.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Here with Ahalya, the sage practised Yoga for thousands of years.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	"O Rama, one day, the sage having gone to a distant place, Indra, finding Ahalya alone, assumed his form, and said to her:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	'O Fair One, I am overcome by desire, let us carry out our conjugal duty.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	"O Raghava, though Ahalya recognized Indra disguised as her lord, yet she acceded to his request.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Then Ahalya addressed Indra saying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	'O Indra, I am highly gratified, now depart quickly, unobserved.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	O Chief of the gods, preserve me and thyself from Gautama.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	"Indra laughed and answered:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	'O You of beautiful waist, to-day I rejoice, I will now depart for my own region.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	On this, he sought to leave the hut of Ahalya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	"O Rama, at that instant he observed the Rishi Gautama entering the hut and he became agitated and anxious.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Seeing the holy sage unconquered by devas or danavas, endowed with the power of Yoga, drenched with holy water, shining like fire, holding the sacred fuel and kusha grass in his hands, Indra was terrified and grew pale.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	"Shri Gautama perceiving Indra in his own guise and judging by his guilty looks that he was leaving his spouse having committed sin with her, cursed him saying:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	"'O Wicked Wretch, assuming my form, you have committed this sinful act.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Be you impotent.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Cursed by the Rishi Gautama, Indra was instantly deprived of his manhood.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Then the Sage Gautama cursed Ahalya also saying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	'You shalt remain immovable in this place for thousands of years, your food the wind alone.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	You shalt be as dust, invisible to all creatures.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	When Rama, the son of Dasaratha visits this forest, then shalt you be cleansed from your sin.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	Having served him, O Deluded One without desire for personal gain, you shalt be restored to me in your present body.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	48_Gautama's hermitage	"Thus did the illustrious Gautama curse the wicked Ahalya and, abandoning the hermitage, began his yogic penances, on the beautiful peak of Himalaya, inhabited by siddhas."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	Deprived of his virility, Indra grew melancholy, and addressing Agni and the other gods, said: "By obstructing the ascetic practices of the Mahatma Gautama, who sought to usurp my power, I have verily served the purpose of the gods.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	Evoking his wrath, by causing him to curse me and denounce Ahalya, I have robbed the rishi of his spiritual power, therefore, O Devas, O Divine Beings, help me now to recover my manhood."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	Then the gods with Agni at their head, approached the pittris, kavyavahanas and other beings and said to them: "Indra has been deprived of his virility; this ram of yours is in full possession of its powers, allow us to graft the testicles of the ram on to Indra, we can compensate the ram in this wise--from to-day, let those who desire to propitiate you, offer the sacrifice of a castrated ram and receive the reward of great merit at your hands."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	The pittris did as requested by Agni and grafted the testicles of the ram on to Indra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	From that time, O Rama, they have accepted the sacrifice of a gelded ram.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	This event proves the immeasurable power of the practices of the holy sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	Now let us enter his hermitage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	O Rama, do you liberate the unfortunate Ahalya, so that she may once more resume her nymph-like form."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	Shri Rama accepted the command and entered the hermitage, preceded by the Sage Vishvamitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	There they beheld Ahalya, by virtue of her yogic practices.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	Unperceived by devas, asuras or men, it seemed as if Brahma had created her with his own hands as a great mistress of occult powers.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	Resembling the full moon veiled in mist or the reflection of the sun in water or a bright fire wreathed in smoke, by the curse of the Rishi Gautama she remained invisible and thus it was ordained she should remain till she beheld Shri Ramacandra and till that hour, none in the three worlds should look on her.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	With the deepest reverence did Shri Rama and Lakshmana touch the feet of Ahalya and she, remembering the words of the Rishi Gautama fell down in devotion before them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	Thereafter, she entertained them with due hospitality, as enjoined in the scriptures, while the two princes acknowledged the honour paid to them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	At this moment a rain of flowers fell from the sky, scattered by the gods; heavenly musicians sang and celestial nymphs danced whilst all rejoiced and paid homage to Ahalya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	The illustrious Sage Gautama becoming aware of the matter through his divine powers, repaired to the hermitage and rejoiced to behold Ahalya restored to her former state.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	Re-united, they both worshipped the glorious Rama and then resumed their spiritual life together.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	49_Shri Rama liberates Ahalya from Gautama's curse	Shri Rama, having accepted the homage offered to him, departed thence for Mithila.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Preceded by Shri Vishvamitra, Shri Rama and Lakshmana came to the king's place of sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Beholding the sacrificial pavilion, they said to the holy sage: "How well has the great Janaka prepared for the sacrifice!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	O August Rishi, thousands of brahmins learned in the Vedas, from many lands, with hundreds of bullock carts transporting their possessions, can be seen here.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	O Holy Father, let us choose a place where you mayest rest."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	The Sage thereupon selected a place which was secluded and supplied with water.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Hearing of the arrival of Shri Vishvamitra, King Janaka, accompanied by his illustrious priest, Shri Shatananda, and many others, hastened to that place and humbly offered obeisance to the holy sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Then the king placed the traditional gifts of water sweetened with honey before him and he, accepting the gifts, enquired as to the king's welfare and further whether the sacrifice was proceeding without hindrance; he then duly inquired concerning the welfare of Shri Shatananda and other holy men in attendance on their sovereign.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	The king received all with a cheerful countenance and with joined palms said to Shri Vishvamitra: "O August Lord, please be seated with the other great sages."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Thus requested, they sat down, after which Janaka with his family priest, brahmins and counsellors occupied their places, the king seated in the midst of his ministers.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Having attended to the due placing of his guests, the illustrious sovereign said: "O Lord, to-day, by the grace of the gods, all the preparations for the sacrifice have been carried out, now by thine advent here I have acquired merit equal to the fruit of my sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Blessed am I that you have honoured the place of sacrifice with your presence.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	O Divine Sage, the high priests have informed me that the sacrifice will be completed in the course of twelve days, the gods will then come to take their share; You, O Illustrious Lord, shalt behold them."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Having thus addressed the sage, the king again earnestly enquired of him, saying: "May prosperity attend you!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	O Sage, who are these two illustrious princes, equalling the gods in power, whose bearing resembles the majesty of an elephant, or a lion, who are valiant and whose eyes are like lotuses, who are armed with swords, bows and quivers and whose beauty rivals the Asvini-Kumara, who are youthful and appear to have descended from heaven to earth like the gods?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Have they come here on foot?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Whose sons are they?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	They, whose eyes are wide set and who are armed with sacred weapons, who wear their hair like Karttikeya and who captivate the hearts of men by their magnanimous and virtuous qualities?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Surely they are come hither to exalt our hearts and add to the fame of our dynasty?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Adorning the earth as the sun or moon adorn the sky, in stature and bearing resembling each other, O Great Sage, whose sons are they?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Please tell me all!"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Hearing the words of King Janaka, Shri Vishvamitra said: "These are the sons of King Dasaratha."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	He then told the king of their residence in the Siddha-Asrama and of the slaying of the demons, of their visit to Vishala and the rescue of Ahalya, also of their meeting with the Sage Gautama.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Then he said: "Now have we come to see the great bow."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	50_The place of sacrifice by King Janaka	Having related all this to the king, the great muni became silent.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Having heard the words of the wise Vishvamitra, Shri Shatananda, the eldest son of the Sage Gautama, resplendent by virtue of his practice of Yoga, was filled with wonder and delight and, beholding Shri Rama was astonished.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Seeing the two princes sitting at their ease, Shri Shatananda said to the Sage Vishvamitra: "O Holy Sage, was my mother, so long involved in the practice of austerity, shown by you to Shri Ramacandra?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	O Illustrious One, did my mother entertain these two heroes worthy of adoration with fruits and those things she was able to obtain in the hermitage?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	"O Holy Rishi, didst you relate the story of the improper behaviour of Indra to my mother in bygone days, to Shri Ramacandra?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	O Holy One, by virtue of the advent of Shri Rama, did my mother obtain my father's favour once more?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	O Kaushika, did my father duly honour Shri Ramacandra and is this Illustrious One, having received the hospitality of my parents, really come hither?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	O Holy Sage, please tell me; when my tranquil-minded sire entered the hermitage, was he honoured by Shri Rama?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Shri Vishvamitra, skilled in the art of converse and acquainted with the laws of rhetoric, answered Shri Shatananda saying:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	"O Great Muni, I did that which should be done, by speaking that which was proper to the occasion, and patiently listening to that which was spoken, recollecting my duty.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	As Jamadagni, who first cursed Renuka and was then reconciled to her, so has your father shown favour to your mother and received her again."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Hearing the words of Shri Vishvamitra, the great Shatananda addressed Shri Ramacandra, saying: "O Great One, may your coming be the source of prosperity to hll.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	It is fortunate indeed that you didst visit my father's hermitage and restore my mother to her former state.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	How can I sufficiently praise that mighty Sage Shri Vishvamitra, reverenced by all the sages.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	O Rama, enlightened are his actions; by virtue of his holy practices he has become a brahmarishi though previously a royal sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Among brahmarishis he is unique, he is known to me as one who is ever concerned with the good of all.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	O Rama, none is equal to you on earth, since you are protected by so great a sage as Vishvamitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Hear while I relate the story of the great Kaushika to you:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	"In the past, this holy sage was a virtuous monarch, versed in all branches of learning, delighting in the welfare of his subjects and the destroyer of his foes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	"Kusha, the righteous and powerful king, was the son of Prajapati, and his son was Gadhi, and the great and illustrious Sage Vishvamitra is the son of Gadhi.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	"On ascending the throne, King Vishvamitra ruled the earth for many thousands of years.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	At a certain time, King Vishvamitra, assembling his army, set out to range the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	O Rama, he passed through many cities and kingdoms and crossed innumerable rivers, mountains and forests, visiting many hermitages till he came to the one belonging to Shri Vasishtha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	This hermitage was thickly planted with many-branched trees with dense foliage in which birds of every kind dwelt.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Many species of beasts frequented that place, and the siddhas also came there--devas, gandharvas and other celestial beings added to the peace and beauty of that hermitage by their presence.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Beautifiil birds flew about and peaceful deer wandered here and there.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Many learned brahmins also dwelt in that hermitage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	"Brahmin sages and also celestial rishis inhabited that place, so that it shone like fire by virtue of their presence.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	This hermitage sheltered many great Vedic scholars equal to Brahma, some living only on air, some on water, some on dry leaves.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Other sages lived on fruit and roots, and there were in addition thousands of brahmacaris fully self-subdued.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	"Each sage observed the sacred traditions, performing his morning and evening devotions, repeating the silent prayer (japa) offering water to the spirits of his ancestors, and pouring oblations into the sacrificial fire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	"Many retired householders practising Yoga, dwelt there with their wives.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	51_Gautama's son Shatananda	Verily that hermitage resembled the abode of Brahma, and the great and powerful King Vishvamitra rejoiced to behold it."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	Beholding the hermitage, the mighty Vishvamitra filled with joy, bowed with great humility to Shri Vasishtha who was engaged in the telling of his rosary.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	'Shri Vasishtha welcomed the king and bade him be seated, and he having done so was offered the fruits and roots that grew in that place.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	'Honoured by the holy sage, King Vishvamitra enquired of him if all were well with the fire sacrifice, his spiritual practices and his disciples.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	Shri Vasishtha related to him all that concerned his welfare and the welfare of those in the hermitage, even to the trees themselves.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	'Sitting at ease, Shri Vasishtha said to King Vishvamitra, eminent among yogis and a son of Shri Brahma himself: "O King, is it well with you in all ways?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	Dost you give satisfaction to your subjects in accordance with the law of righteousness and dost you rule and protect your people according to the spiritual law?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	Is your revenue justly received and increased?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	Is it judiciously administered and distributed to those who are eligible and deserving?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	Are your servants remunerated at the proper season?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	Do your subjects willingly obey you?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	O Sovereign, hast you subdued thine enemies?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	O Sinless King, is it well with thine army, your treasury, your friends, your sons and grandsons?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	'In reply to these questions, King Vishvamitra humbly answered: "All is well, my Lord!"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	'Conversing pleasantly together for a long time, recounting the ancient traditions to each other, they thus promoted their mutual delight.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	'O Prince of the House of Raghu, when King Vishvamitra paused, Shri Vasishtha said to him smilingly: "O King, although you have with you a large retinue, yet it is my desire to offer you hospitality, together with thine army.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	Be pleased to accept it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	Since you are a distinguished guest, it is meet that I should do all within my power to entertain you, therefore, be gracious enough to receive the little I have to offer."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	'King Vishvamitra answered: "O Lord, your gentle and pleasing words are sufficient entertainment.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	Moreover, you have already presented me with fruits and the clear water of your hermitage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	By meeting with you alone, am I sufficiently honoured.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	O Supremely Wise One, it was proper that I should offer obeisance to you; now you have entertained me, allow me to offer you salutations and depart."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	'The great sage declined to accept the king's refusal of his offer, and still insisted that he should entertain him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	'Then Vishvamitra said: "Be it according to your pleasure, my Lord, I will do as you desirest."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	'At these words, Shri Vasishtha sent for his favourite spotted cow Kamadhenu and said to her: "O Shabala, draw near and listen to me, I desire to offer hospitality to the king and his army.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	52_King Vishvamitra visits Shri Vasishtha's hermitage	O Dear One, you are the wish-fulfilling cow and can accomplish anything, therefore, now prepare splendid dishes which will be pleasing to them, of the six kinds of taste.1 Produce speedily whatever food can be eaten, drunk, licked or sucked."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	The cow Shabala provided for the needs of all according to the instruction of Shri Vasishtha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	Sugar cane, sweets of various kinds, honey, crushed barley, wine and other excellent drinks, hot rice in heaps as high as mountains, milk, curry and other fare combining the six tastes and countless other dishes with sweets made of jagari were distributed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	Each was wholly satisfied and delighted with the hospitality of Shri Vasishtha, who accorded to all the companions and retainers of King Vishvamitra the full extent of their desires.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	The king with his family priests, ministers and attendants, partaking of the feast offered with generosity and respect by the great sage, was highly gratified.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	When all the counsellors and personal attendants and the army had received full hospitality, the king, wholly satisfied, said to Shri Vasishtha: "O Holy Sage, you have entertained me royally, please hear what I have to say O Eloquent One!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	O Lord, give me the cow Shabala in exchange for a hundred thousand excellent cows.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	Shabala is a jewel and by a king should jewels be enjoyed--according to the natural law, this treasure should therefore be mine."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	Shri Vasishtha answered, saying: "O King, I will not part with Shabala in exchange for ten million cows, still less for a hundred thousand.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	If you did'st offer me mountains of silver yet would I refuse to give you Shabala for she must remain in my hermitage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	"O King, as a righteous man cares for his good name, so do I for Shabala.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	She helps me to satisfy the devas, the pittris and other beings.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	My sacred fire sacrifice and other Vedic rites, besides the various branches of learning depend on Shabala.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	O Great Ruler, indeed I cannot relinquish this cow, she is my all and she fulfils all my needs--for these and numerous other reasons do I refuse to yield the cow to you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	O King, verily I will not part with Shabala."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	The words of Shri Vasishtha merely increased the king's desire and he, under great emotion, declared with passion: "O Great Muni, I will give you fourteen thousand elephants adorned with golden trappings, ornaments and goads and, in addition, I will give you a hundred and eight chariots made of solid gold, each driven by four milk white horses.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	At the same time, I offer you eleven thousand well-trained horses, each with a golden harness and further ten million cows of varied colours, that are young and healthy.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	O give me Shabala, and I will give you in exchange as much gold as you desirest.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	Grant me Shabala, I implore you, and accept my gifts, O Sage."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	Then the wise Vasishtha said: "Under no condition can I part with Shabala, O King, she is my jewel and my wealth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	She is my very life, my all-in-all, and she furnishes me with alms and all I require for sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	53_King Vishvamitra desires to possess Shabala	In brief, O King, Shabala is the source of my spiritual life and I will never give her up."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	O Rama, perceiving that Shri Vasishtha would not willingly consent to part with the cow, Vishvamitra resolved to carry her away by force.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	O Raghava, while Shabala was being forcibly carried off, distracted with grief, she began to reflect thus: "Why has the holy Vasishtha abandoned me?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	In what way have I offended the holy sage?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Why are the servants of the king dragging me away from the hermitage?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	lam innocent and docile, the holy muni is dear to me; what fault have I committed that the Mahatma Vasishtha should abandon me?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Sighing again and again, Shabala, shaking off the hands of the king's attendants, swiftly ran and placed her head at the feet of the holy sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Standing before Shri Vasishtha, shedding tears and lamenting loudly, she cried: "O Lord, O Son of Brahma hast you verily abandoned me?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Why are the servants of the king taking me away from your presence, by force?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Seeing the sorely stricken Shabala, Shri Vasishtha addressed her as he would his own sister, saying: "O Shabala, it is not by my will that you are thus being carried away, neither hast you offended me in any way, O Dear One.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Drunk with desire, the king is taking you from me by force.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	I have not the power to defend you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	The king is a warrior and lord of the earth, he is attended by a mighty army with horses, elephants and chariots, verily he is mightier than I."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Shabala, who was skilled in argument, listened to the words of Shri Vasishtha and said: "O Holy Sage, the power of a warrior is as nought compared to that of a holy sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	O Illustrious Lord, the strength of a sage is divine and based on the exercise of spiritual practices and discipline, it is therefore limitless; you are, O Lord, immeasurably stronger than a kshatriya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	The power of that mighty king Vishvamitra, is great, but he cannot equal your strength and splendour.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	O Lord, through your strength and energy suffer me to destroy the power and pride of this wicked wretch."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Shri Vasishtha answered: "Be it so!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Create an army by your spiritual energy, that will destroy the forces of the king."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Lowing loudly, Shabala, in obedience to the sage, instantly produced hundreds of foreign soldiers, who began to destroy the army of Vishvamitra while he was looking on.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Perceiving his army about to be overthrown, King Vishvamitra became enraged and, mounting his chariot, his eyes red with anger, he advanced to the attack.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	With various weapons, he began to slay thousands of men, and Shabala, seeing the army created by her, annihilated, now produced strange beings called shakas in such numbers, that they filled the whole earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Highly valorous, their skins shining like gold, clad in yellow armour, furnished with scimitars and maces, they started to consume the army of Vishvamitra like a raging fire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	54_King Vishvamitra attempts to carry Shabala away by force	Then the great Vishvamitra, with the aid of yogic weapons, began to create disorder in the ranks of the forces produced by Shabala.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	As the mighty warriors fell, pierced by the weapons of Vishvamitra's forces, Shri Vasishtha said to Shabala: "O Shabala, create more warriors by the power of Yoga."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Shabala, lowing loudly, produced well-armed soldiers from her feet and udders, and from her hair and thighs were born the extraordinary warriors Harita and Kirata.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	By these, the whole army of Vishvamitra consisting of elephants, horses and chariots, was instantly destroyed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Beholding their entire army exterminated by the power of Shri Vasishtha, King Vishvami-tra's hundred sons bearing mighty arms and with various thought-propelled weapons rushed angrily at the holy Sage Vasishtha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Shri Vasishtha merely uttered the sound "H'm!"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	and they were all immediately consumed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	By the great Sage Vasishtha, the infantry, cavalry and chariots, together with the sons of King Vishvamitra, were instantly burned to ashes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Then the illustrious monarch Vishvamitra whose sons and army had been annihilated, was filled with shame and dismay.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Deprived of his glory, he resembled a waveless ocean or a snake bereft of its fangs or the sun under eclipse.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Like a bird without wings, his confidence shattered, his pride humbled, he became filled with anxiety.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Bestowing the kingdom on his only remaining son, he exhorted him to rule according to dharma and then himself retired to the forest to practise asceticism.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	After some time, he found favour with Shri Mahadeva the magnanimous granter of boons, and he, appearing before Vishvamitra, addressed him saying: "O King, why art you undergoing penance?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	What is your desire?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	I will grant you whatsoever you asks?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Shri Vishvamitra making obeisance to Shri Mahadeva said to him: "O Great God, if I have found favour with you, then instruct me in the Upanishads and other branches of learning, teach me also the mysteries and the science of archery.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Whatever weapons are known to the danavas, yakshas, asuras and other beings, let them be revealed to me by your grace."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	On hearing the request of the king, Shri Shiva answered, "Be it so" and returned to his abode.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	King Vishvamitra, having acquired the various weapons from Mahadeva, became as happy as the sea at the time of the full moon.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	He now resolved to subdue the Sage Vasishtha and regarded him as his captive already.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Proceeding to his hermitage he discharged his great weapons like rain, setting the forest of Tapovan ablaze.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Afflicted by these dreadful weapons, all the sages began to flee to the four quarters in terror; even the disciples of Shri Vasishtha, together with innumerable birds and beasts, escaped hastily in every direction.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	The hermitage of Shri Vasishtha became deserted and a deep silence fell upon it, causing it to resemble a barren field.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Shri Vasishtha repeatedly called out: "Fear not, fear not, I will destroy Vishvamitra as the sun dispels the morning mist."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Then the great Sage Vasishtha, foremost among those who practise silent prayer, angrily addressed Vishvamitra saying: "You have destroyed my ancient and auspicious hermitage, O Wicked and Deluded Wretch, you thyself shaft be destroyed."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	55_Shabala creates an army which annihilates Vishvamitra's forces	Snatching up his staff equal to the rod of Yama, he advanced like a naked flame.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	Hearing the harsh words uttered by Shri Vasishtha, Vishvamitra raising the fire weapon, cried: "Stay!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	Beware!"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	Then Shri Vasishtha, lifting up his Brahma staff in wrath, exclaimed: "O Vilest of Warriors, here I stand, let loose all your weapons, not excepting those propelled by thought which you have obtained from the Lord Shiva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	O Son of Gadhi, to-day I will deprive you of all these weapons.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	How can your power as a warrior compare with that of a divine sage?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	O Stupid Wretch, behold my divine energy!"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	So saying, Shri Vasishtha quenched the dangerous fire weapon hurled at him by Vishvamitra as water quenches fire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	Then the son of Gadhi let fly other dangerous weapons upon the holy sage, the Varuna, the Rudra, the Indra, the Pashupata and Ishika weapons together with the Manava, Mohana, Gandharva, Swapana, Jrimbhana, Viadana, Santapana, and Vilapana; the Shoshana, Darana and the terrible Vatra; the Brahmapasha and Kalapasha, the Varunapasha and the priceless Pinaka and also the missiles Shushka and Ardra, the Danda weapon and the Pisacha, the Krouncha and the Dharmadiscus, the Kala discus and the discus of Vishnu, also the weapon Vayuvya, Mathana and Haya-shira did he discharge upon the great sage with the two Shaktis, the Kankala, Mushala, Vidyadhara, Kala, the trident Kapala and the Kankana.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	All these did he hurl at the holy sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	Then Shri Vasishtha accomplished a great marvel and by means of his staff alone destroyed all the weapons of Vishvamitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	Seeing these weapons rendered ineffectual, Vishvamitra raised the Brahman-astra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	At this, Agni, the divine sages and the celestial beings were seized with terror and the three worlds shook with fear.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	But by means of his spiritual power and the study and practice of Brahman-Vidya, Shri Vasishtha subdued the Brahman-astra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	As Shri Vasishtha consumed this tremendous weapon, his charming and pleasing mien became terrible and from each pore of his body shafts of light shot forth while the staff of the holy sage, shining like fire, burst into flame.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	All the sages now began to praise Shri Vasishtha, saying: "Your power is without equal and ever productive of good, by the power of your Yoga, pacify the Brahman-astra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	O Holy Sage, you have humbled the pride of Vishvamitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	O Great Ascetic, be pacified, that we also may be delivered from fear."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	Thus addressed, Shri Vasishtha assumed his accustomed mien and Vishvamitra, being defeated, sighing heavily, exclaimed: "Woe, woe to the might of a warrior!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	The real power is the spiritual power.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	Shri Vasishtha by his spiritual strength has fully conquered mine.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	56_Shri Vasishtha conquers Vishvamitra	I will, therefore, abandon my warlike nature and seek to obtain brahmanhood."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	The heart of Vishvamitra was heavy, remembering his disgrace, and he was filled with remorse at having borne enmity to Shri Vasishtha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	O Rama, with his queen he went to the southern quarter and began his great ascetic penance there.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	After a long time four sons were born to him, each a devotee of truth, who were virtuous and of great military prowess.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	Their names were Havisyanda, Madhusyanda, Drirha-netra and Maharatha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	Having practised severe austerities for a thousand years, the Grandsire of the world, Shri Brahma appeared before Vishvamitra and said: "O Son of Kaushika, you have surpassed the royal sages in your great asceticism, you shalt, therefore, be numbered among them."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	Having thus spoken, Shri Brahma with the gods went to Brahmaloka.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	Vishvamitra was filled with shame and with bowed head, overcome with grief, thus spoke: "Alas!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	In spite of prolonged austerities, the gods still hold me to be a royal sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	I deem this state no reward for the penance I have undergone."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	O Rama, with renewed resolve, Vishvamitra, pre-eminent in the field of endeavour began his life of mortification anew.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	At this time, the great King Trishanku of the House of Ikswaku, fully self-subdued and a lover of truth, resolved to initiate a sacrifice in order to enter heaven in his physical body.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	Summoning the holy Sage Vasishtha, he communicated his intention to him, but the Mahatma Vasishtha, having duly considered the matter, said: "O King, this cannot be."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	Discouraged by Shri Vasishtha and for the purpose of fulfilling his design, the monarch went southwards to where the sons of Shri Vasishtha abode, leading lives of purity and ascetism.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	When King Trishanku beheld the sons of his own Guru, that great and illustrious sage, he was full of shame, and with bowed head offered salutation to them, addressing them in great humility saying, "O Protectors of those who seek refuge in you, I come to seek your aid.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	O Holy Ones, I besought your sire to assist me in the observance of a sacrifice and he discouraged me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	I have, therefore, come to seek your help in the matter.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	O Sons of my Holy Guru, I offer salutations to you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	Again and again, I bow down to you, O Holy Ones, and beseech you to officiate at the proposed sacrifice, which I desire to undertake for the fulfilment of my design, namely that I may ascend to heaven in my embodied state.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	Discouraged by the holy teacher Vasishtha, I consider that you alone are able to assist me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	Should you refuse me, there is none in whom I may take refuge.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	57_Shri Vasishtha refuses to help King Trishanku	The kings of the House of Ikshvaku have always sought guidance of their spiritual preceptor in time of need, and the holy and learned Sage Vasishtha has ever upheld the dynasty and, following him, you alone are my instructors
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	O Rama, hearing the words of the king, the hundred sons of Shri Vasishtha were filled with wrath and said: "O You Evil-minded Wretch, discouraged by your spiritual preceptor, how dost you dare to seek our aid?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	O King, we know you to be an ignorant man.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	Shri Vasishtha is able to advance the sacrifices of the three worlds, verily you are no true disciple of such a sage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	Shall we render void the utterance of our great sire?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	Hearing these harsh words, the king replied: "Discouraged by my Guru and now by you, I shall seek elsewhere for aid; may all be well with you."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	The sons of the great sage were enraged on hearing these words spoken in defiance, and cursed the king, saying: "Mayest you become one of the fallen caste."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	Having thus cursed him, they returned to their hermitage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	When the night was over, the king was transformed into a low-born being, his complexion dark, his body emaciated, his head shaven, his whole frame besmeared with ashes from the crematorium, his golden ornaments changed to lead.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	When the people of the capital beheld the king in this condition they fled from that place, and Trishanku departed, full of anguish.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	Sunk in grief day and night, he finally sought refuge with Shri Vishvamitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	That sage seeing the monarch deprived of his kingdom and condemned to assume the form of a low-caste being, was moved with compassion, and addressed him saying: "O Mighty Prince, mayest you be prosperous!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	Why hast you come hither?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	I know you to be the Sovereign of Ayodhya that through a curse art come to this state."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	The eloquent King Trishanku, with joined palms, replied in tones of submission: "O Great One, discouraged by my Guru and his sons in my desire to enter heaven in the physical body, I have been transformed by them into a chandala.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	Now, for shame, I may not show myself to any.
