RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	O Lord, I have failed to obtain the fruit of countless sacrifices, an untruth has never been uttered by me, I have governed my people with righteousness and by my conduct have satisfied my spiritual preceptor and holy men.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	I desired to undertake a further meritorious sacrifice, but O Great Sage, my Guru has withheld his aid.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	O Lord, destiny is irrevocable, destiny is inexorable, none can withstand it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	All are ruled by destiny.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	O Divine Sage, be favourable to me, who am fallen into distress!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	Besides you, there is none in whom I can take refuge.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	58_Vasishtha's sons curse Trishanku	O Holy One, by your spiritual energy, avert this evil fate."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	Shri Vishvamitra heard the appeal of the fallen sovereign and in sweet accents spoke words of comfort, saying: "O King, you are welcome, I know you to be wholly virtuous, I will be your refuge, fear not.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	I shall invite hither the learned and pious brahmans who will assist you in the performance of your sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	This you shalt accomplish and obtain heaven in the form imposed on you by your Guru.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	O King, having taken refuge in me, consider your purpose already accomplished."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	Having uttered these words, Shri Vishvamitra commanded his sons to prepare all things for the sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	Summoning his disciples, he said to them: "Bring hither the pious and learned brahmins and the sons of Shri Vasishtha also.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	May they come with their disciples, their friends, the learned and the priests.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	If any disregard my word, let it be reported to me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	In obedience to the sage, the disciples set out to every quarter, summoning the sages and learned men from many lands.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	Returning, they approached Vishvamitra, and said: "O Lord, at your command the holy sages are coming hither, some are already come, Mahodeva excepted; but the sons of holy Vasishtha, transported with rage uttered harsh words of which we will tell you."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	They said: "How shall divine sages partake of that sacrifice undertaken by a chandala, at which a kshatriya officiates?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	And how shall those brahmins, constrained by Vishvamitra, partaking of the food offered by a chandala, enter heaven?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	O Great Sage, these are the words of the sons of Shri Vasishtha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	Vishvamitra, his eyes red with anger, answered: "Why should the sons of Shri Vasishtha disregard me, who am engaged in severe ascetic practices and without guilt?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	By my power, these evil-minded men shall this day be consumed to ashes and enter the abode of death.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	By my curse they shall become of those who subsist on the dead for a hundred incarnations.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	They shall eat the flesh of dogs and be called 'Musthika'.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	Despised by all, they shall wander about among men and may the wicked Mahodeva also, having imputed blame to me, be born as a fowler, for a long time becoming the pitiless destroyer of other's lives and by my wrath may he sink to a miserable and abject state."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	59_Vishvamitra seeks the help of the sons of Vasishtha and Mahodeva	Sitting amid the sages, the Sage Vishvamitra having pronounced this curse, became silent.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	Having stricken the sons of Shri Vasishtha by the power of his asceticism, Vishvamitra, seated amidst the sages, spoke:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'"The renowned monarch Trishanku of the dynasty of Ikshvaku, who is both magnanimous and virtuous, has taken refuge with me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	He is desirous of entering heaven in his embodied state, it is for me to accomplish it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	O Sages, do you unitedly assist him in this sacrifice."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'The sages hearing the words of Vishvamitra and being acquainted with the tradition, consulted together saying: "The son of Kaushika, the Rishi Vishvamitra, is given to wrath.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	If we do not fulfil his desire, like a consuming fire he will pour out his curse upon us.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	Let us, therefore, assist him in the sacrifice so that the king may enter heaven in his physical body.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	Now let us inaugurate the rites."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'Then the rites began, as prescribed by ancient tradition, Vishvamitra acting as the chief priest and the learned brahmins becoming the sacrificing priests subordinate to him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	Observing numerous rituals, the sacrifice continued for a long time.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	Then Shri Vishvamitra called thither the gods for their share of the sacrifice, but none of these celestial beings appeared.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	At this the great sage grew exceedingly wroth and lifting up the sacrificial vessel, said to the King Trishanku: "O King, behold the power of my asceticism by virtue of which I now send you to heaven in your embodied state.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	O King, though it is deemed impossible to accomplish this, by the power acquired by me I now say to you; 'ascend to heaven in your physical form.'"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'Having uttered these words, King Trishanku, in the presence of the sages instantly ascended to the heavens.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'Seeing Trishanku there, Indra and all the other gods exclaimed: "O Trishanku, you have no place in heaven.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	Cursed by your Guru, O Stupid Wretch, do you fall headlong to the earth."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'Trishanku accordingly instantly began to fall towards the earth crying out to Shri Vishvamitra, "Protect me", "Protect me".
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'Shri Vishvamitra, hearing the cry, grew angry, and called out, "Stay, Stay".
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	At that moment, standing amidst the sages, the great rishi resembled Prajapati.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	Thereafter he created seven planets in the southern quarter called the Seven Rishis, and then he created the Ashvini and twenty-seven other stars.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	Seated amidst the sages, filled with wrath, Vishvamitra reflected in himself: "I will create another Indra or I will leave this heaven without an Indra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	Nay, I will make Trishanku Lord of this heaven," and he began to create a new circle of gods.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'Upon this, the sages, gods and celestial beings, bewildered and perturbed, approached Vishvamitra and said with humility: "O Great Sage, this king has been cursed by his spiritual preceptor and is not worthy of heaven."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'Shri Vishvamitra answered them, saying: "Hear, O you Gods, I have vowed that this king should enter heaven in his embodied state, this pledge must be fulfilled.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	To this end, I have created the Pole star and other planets and this heaven will abide as long as the former heaven endures, as also the gods created by me, it becomes you, therefore, to confirm what I have promised."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'The gods in awe, having heard these words, answered: "Be it so, O Illustrious Rishi, the heaven created by you shall endure beyond the Path of Vishvanara, and let Trishanku, suspended head downwards, remain as if immortal among these shining stars.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	As the stars attend on famous and successful men, so let these brilliant luminaries, created by you, attend on King Trishanku."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'Shri Vishvamitra, extolled by the gods, acquiesced in their proposal.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	60_King Trishanku ascends to a specially created heaven	'After this, O Rama, the gods and the ascetics who had attended the sacrifice, returned to their own regions.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	O Rama, when Vishvamitra saw the sages departing, he said to the dwellers of the Tapovana forest: "In the southern region, great obstructions have hindered my penances, I shall therefore go to another quarter to perform austerity.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	To the west of this place, at the sacred spot named Pushkara, there is a large and beautiful forest where I shall continue my practices undisturbed."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	Reaching that place, the great sage engaging in occult practices, subsisted on fruit and roots.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	Meanwhile, King Ambarisha of Ayodhya inaugurated the horse sacrifice, but the horse was carried away by Indra, on which the priest addressed the monarch, saying: "O King, it is for you to protect the sacrificial steed, the horse has been stolen away owing to your negligence, therefore, provide another or seek a human victim, so that the sacrifice may be accomplished without further hindrance."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	Hearing these words, the renowned monarch offered thousands of cows to whosoever should find either a horse, or human being.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	Seeking the sacrificial beast, the illustrious sovereign passed through many countries, cities and forests, and entered hermitages and sacred places.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	At length, the King Ambarisha beheld Richika the Sage, with his sons and wife dwelling on the mountain Bhrigutunga.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	Making obeisance to him, the king honoured him in various ways and enquired as to his welfare.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	He then said to him: "If it be agreeable to you, grant me one of your sons in exchange for a hundred thousand cows.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	After searching many countries, I have not found either a horse or a human victim for the sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	O Lord, do you, therefore, deliver your son to me and accede to my request."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	Richika answered: "O King, I will never bestow my eldest son on any."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	His wife then said: "My Lord does not wish to part with the eldest son, but the youngest son Shunaka is dearest to me, I shall not part with him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	O Great Muni, the eldest son is beloved of his father and the youngest is dear to his mother, therefore, these two should not be taken away."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	O Rama, the middle son, whose name was Shunashepha, hearing these words, spoke thus: "My father does not wish to part with his eldest son, nor my mother with her youngest, therefore, take me, O King."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	61_King Ambarisha's sacrificial horse is lost	O Rama, the king gave the Sage Richika a hundred thousand cows in exchange for Shunashepha and, mounting his chariot, started with him on his homeward journey.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	O Rama, the illustrious King Ambarisha, accompanied by Shunashepha, having in the afternoon reached Pushkara, rested there.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	While the king rested, Shunashepha, going to a certain spot, beheld Shri Vishvamitra, his maternal uncle, engaged with other sages in the performance of spiritual practices and he, sorrowful, thirsty and fatigued, fell at the feet of the sage, and said: "O Lord, for me there is neither father, mother, relative nor caste.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	O Peaceful Sage, O Sovereign among ascetics, I take refuge in you; in the name of dharma, deliver me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	You can'st protect the whole world, how much more one so insignificant as myself.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	Do you assist the king in the completion of his sacrifice that it may be accomplished without hindrance, and may I live and by means of my spiritual practices obtain heaven.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	You are my master who am masterless.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	Protect me, wretched as I am, as a father protects his child."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	'Shri Vishvamitra, hearing the piteous words of Shunashepha addressed his own sons, saying: "O My Sons, that world for which fathers beget their children is at hand, this child is the son of the Sage Richika and has taken refuge in me, let us protect his life.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	You are all virtuous and charitable, let one of you take the place of the sacrificial victim at the king's sacrifice, and thus satisfy the God Agni.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	In this way, we can rescue Shunashepha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	Assist me in the completion of the king's sacrifice, propitiate the gods, and enable me to be true to my word."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	'Hearing these words, Madhusyanda and the other sons sullenly replied to Vishvamitra, saying: "O King of Kings, would'st you abandon thine own sons and protect another's?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	Such an action resembles the relinquishing of a tasty dish to partake of the flesh of a dog."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	'Hearing this reply, Shri Vishvamitra grew angry and, his eyes inflamed with wrath, he said: "Your speech is arrogant and contrary to dharma, it is a violation of filial affection.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	I regard you all as insubordinate, therefore, I now curse you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	Like the sons of Shri Vasishtha, may you fall from your high caste and, eating the flesh of dogs, wander about in the world during the period of a thousand years!"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	'Having thus cursed his sons, the muni, offering Shunashepha his protection, thus instructed him: "O Son of a Sage, at King Ambarisha's sacrifice, allow thyself to be bound, adorned with the red garland, besmeared with sandalwood paste and tied to the sacrificial post.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	I will impart to you two mantrams, which when repeated, will deliver you."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	'The holy sage then carefully instructed him in the sacred formulas.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	Thereafter, Shunashepha approached the king and said: "O Illustrious Monarch, now enter upon the initiation without delay and accomplish the performance of your sacrifice."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	'The king, filled with joy, went without delay to the sacrificial pavilion.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	With the consent of the officiating priest, the king now dressed Shunashepha in red attire and tied him to the post as the consecrated victim.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	Being bound, Shunashepha began to praise Upendra by reciting the mantrams he had been given by Vishvamitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	'Indra, pleased with the worship of Shunashepha, bestowed the blessing of long life on him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	'O Rama, then did the king complete his sacrifice and obtain the desired fruit from Indra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	62_Shunashepha obtains help from Vishvamitra	'Thereafter, the righteous Vishvamitra renewed his yogic penance in Pushkara and performed it there for a thousand years.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Shri Vishvamitra passed a thousand years in the practice of mortification, then the gods came to bestow on him the fruits of his asceticism.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	The supreme Brahma addressed him in pleasing accents, saying: "O Holy One, mayest you be prosperous, you are now become a rishi by virtue of your great austerities."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Having said this, Shri Brahma and the other celestial beings returned to their own spheres.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Vishvamitra again engaged in severe austerity and in this way passed many more years.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	While thus employed, the celestial nymph Menaka came to bathe in the Pushkara lake.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Resembling lightning illumining a cloud, her beauty stirred the passion of Vishvamitra and he said to her:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	"Be gracious to me for I am filled with a great love for you."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Then that beautiful one agreed to take up her abode in the hermitage of the rishi'.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	The penances of Vishvamitra were thus rendered void by the presence of Menaka in the hermitage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	O Rama, that nymph passed ten years in that place.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	After this time, Shri Vishvamitra perceiving himself to have been deluded, was filled with shame and he reflected on the cause of his infatuation.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Then he adjudged the gods to have devised this plan to bring his ascetism to nought and he cried out: "What, have I passed ten years with this woman, as it were a night.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Alas!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	My great austerities are destroyed by this passion."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Sighing heavily and filled with remorse, he beheld Menaka trembling with fear, standing near, but Vishvamitra addressing her in reassuring words, bade her farewell.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Having controlled his passions, Shri Vishvamitra went to the northern mountains and began to perform penance in the Himalayas on the bank of the Kaushiki river.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Then, O Rama, the gods were filled with fear by the austerities practised by the rishi on the Himalayan mountains, and approaching Shri Brahma said:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	"O Grandsire, now grant the title of maharishi to Shri Vishvamitra."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Shri Brahma then appeared before Vishvamitra and in gentle accents said to him: "Hail to You, O Rishi, I am pleased with thine austerity.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	I name you chief among the rishis."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Then Vishvamitra, making obeisance to Shri Brahma, spoke submissively saying: "O Lord, these penances have been undertaken by me that I might become a brahmarishi.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Since you still namest me maharishi, I regard myself as not yet fully self-subdued."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Shri Brahma answered, saying: "So it is, you have not yet fully gained the mastery over your senses.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	O Great Muni, undergo further penance."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Having uttered these words, Shri Brahma returned to the celestial regions.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Then Vishvamitra began an exceedingly severe penance, standing unsupported with his arms raised, living only on air; in the summer season, standing in the midst of five fires, in the rainy season lying without a canopy, in the winter practising his spiritual discipline in water, thus did he pass a thousand years.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	Perceiving Vishvamitra undergoing these severe penances, the gods were greatly perturbed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	63_Vishvamitra is proclaimed a Maharishi	At length their lord, Indra, approached the nymph Rambha and begged her to promote his interest and cause harm to Vishvamitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	Indra thus addressed Rambha saying: "O Rambha, it is for you to accomplish this great work and stimulate the passions of the great Sage Vishvamitra, so that his spiritual practices may be rendered void."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	O Rama, Rambha, filled with apprehension on hearing the words of Indra, said in humility: "O Indra, the Rishi Vishvamitra is easily moved to wrath, he will certainly curse me if I approach him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	I fear to enter his presence, do not therefore ask me to undertake this task."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	To Rambha, trembling with fear, standing with joined palms, in token of submission, Indra made answer: "O Rambha, fear not, accomplish my desire, may success attend you!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	In the spring season, assuming the form of a cuckoo calling sweetly, accompanied by the god of love, I will take my place on a blossoming tree not far from you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	O Rambha, attired in beautiful and charming apparel do you divert the mind of the muni from his spiritual practices."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	At the instance of Indra, that lovely nymph clad in enchanting raiment, faintly smiling, went forth to allure the heart of Shri Vishvamitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	At that moment, the liquid notes of the cuckoo began to delight the rishi and he then beheld the nymph Rambha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	Stirred by the cuckoo's note and the ravishing sound of the beautiful Rambha's song, Shri Vishvamitra, recollecting his former fall, was filled with misgiving and recognizing the design of the god Indra, transported with rage, cursed Rambha, saying:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	"O Rambha, O Unfortunate One, you have come hither to lure me from my penance, I, who have conquered lust and anger.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	Mayest you become petrified and take the form of a rock for ten thousand years.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	A brahmin perfected in the power of Yoga shall one day deliver you from this curse."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	Having pronounced this curse on Rambha, the rishi became a prey to remorse, for, giving way to wrath he lost the fruit of all his yogic practices.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	Rambha having been instantly turned to stone, Indra and Kama, perceiving the sage filled with wrath, fled in terror.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	Shri Vishvamitra having lost the merit of his penances could obtain no peace; his passions remaining unsubdued, he resolved to speak no word to any and never give way to anger; he said: "For a thousand years, I will not breathe.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	Reducing my body to the last extremity, mastering my senses, I will obtain brahmanhood by the power of my penance.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	Measureless years, shall I remain standing, neither breathing nor eating, even should my limbs become atrophied."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	64_Indra sends Rambha	O Rama, Vishvamitra resolved to perform this mortification for the space of a thousand years.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	After this the great Rishi Vishvamitra, leaving the northern quarter, went eastward and engaged in a most severe course of austerities.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Observing silence for a thousand years, he performed incomparable ascetic practices, hardly able to be accomplished.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	After a thousand years, his form reduced to the semblance of wood, the royal sage, under the greatest provocation, was not incited to anger.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	O Rama, when Vishvamitra was persuaded that he had conquered anger, his vow of a thousand years' mortification being terminated, he sat down to eat.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	At that time, Indra appeared in the guise of a brahmin and requested the food set before the muni, upon which Vishvamitra, believing him to be a sage, gave him the whole which he had prepared for himself and still observing the vow of silence, uttered no word.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	' The chief of the sages, suspending his breath for a further thousand years, continued his penance, then there issued from his head a smoke which terrified the beings of the three worlds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	By the power of his mortification, the devas, gandharvas, and other beings were deprived of their glory and lost consciousness.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	In distress, they addressed Shri Brahma saying: "O Lord, by every means in our power, we have sought to distract the great sage from his penances and provoke him to anger, but he has persisted in his practices and is free from desire and aversion.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	If you dost not grant him brahmanhood, verily the three worlds will be destroyed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	None can find rest anywhere, the seas are drying up and the mountains are riven by the power of his austerities; the sun is deprived of its splendour, the earth is agitated and the wind stirs not.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	O Lord, we cannot move him from his resolve.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	On account of this peril, men like atheists have given up the performance of charitable deeds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Nowhere is peace to be found.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	O Divine Being, lest the mighty Vishvamitra, resplendent as fire, determine to destroy the universe, deign to grant him his desire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	As Time, in the form of fire, at the dissolution of the world, consumes the whole universe, so also will the Sage Vishvamitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Grant him, therefore, Indrahood, if he so desire it, for if You withhold brahmanhood which he has sought to acquire, then only the sovereignty of Indra's region, will content him."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Thus approached, Shri Brahma, accompanied by the gods, appeared before Shri Vishvamitra and in pleasing accents addressed him, saying: "O Brahmarishi, reverence to you, we are pleased with thine austerity.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	O Holy Vishvamitra, by the power of your penance, you have acquired brahmanhood.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	The gods bless you, may prosperity attend you, may longevity be thine I From to-day, you are free, now go where you pleases."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Offering salutations to Shri Brahma and all the gods, Shri Vishvamitra said: "Having bestowed brahmanhood and longevity upon me, grant me instruction in the holy syllable 'aum' and the Vedas also, and further invest me with the authority to officiate at the sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	O You Gods, let the son of Brahma, Shri Vasishtha, fully acquainted with the Vedic science, acknowledge me as a brahmarishi.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	If this desire of mine be fulfilled, you may all depart."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Thereupon the gods appeared before Shri Vasishtha, who having acquiesced in their wish and sealed his friendship with Vishvamitra, said to him: "Verily you are now a brahmarishi and as such I acknowledge you."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Thereafter the gods returned to their own region.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Thus did the illustrious Sage Vishvamitra acquire brahmanhood.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	The divine sage then paid homage to the great Vasishtha and, his purpose accomplished, wandered about the earth engaged in charitable deeds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Shri Shatananda said: "O Rama, this is the story of Shri Vishvamitra and how he obtained brahmanhood.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	O Raghava, verily he is the chief of sages and the personification of Yoga.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Constantly engaged in acts of virtue, he still performs rigorous penances."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Having uttered these words, Shri Shatananda became silent.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	When this excellent sage had ended his narrative, King Janaka in the presence of Rama and Lakshmana humbly addressed Shri Vishvamitra saying: "O Chief of Sages, blessed am I, that you are come with Shri Rama and Lakshmana to my sacrifice.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	O Muni, you have, by your presence, done us great honour.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	O Brahmarishi, you have added to our renown.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Shri Rama, my counsellors and I have heard the story of your wonderful austerities and also of thine excellent qualities.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	O Great Sage, immense is your power, unimaginable your penances, incalculable your virtues, nor does one ever tire of hearing of your marvellous deeds.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	O Illustrious Lord, the sun has set and the time of evening devotion is near, graciously grant us leave to depart; in the morning we shall see you again."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Shri Vishvamitra gratified by the king's words, praised him and granted him permission to depart, upon which King Janaka rose and circumambulating the great sage took his departure, accompanied by his spiritual preceptor and relatives.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	65_Vishvamitra performs another thousand years' austerities	Honoured by the sages, the great Vishvamitra with Shri Rama and Lakshmana also returned to his abode.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	The day dawned peacefully and King Janaka, having performed his morning devotions, called for the two princes and Vishvamitra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	Having honoured the sage and the two descendants of the House of Raghu, he said: "O Blessed Lord, peace be with you, what service can I render you, I am wholly thine."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	Thus addressed by the king, the Sage replied: "These two princes are the sons of King Dasaratha, they are renowned in the warrior caste and exalted throughout the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	They desire to see the great bow, which is deposited with you, be gracious enough to permit them to view it and having thus accomplished their purpose, they will return to their own capital."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	Thus addressed, King Janaka replied to the sage: "O Holy Rishi, hear from me for what reason this bow is deposited with me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	There was a king named Devarata in the sixth generation of the monarch Nimi who obtained this bow as a trust.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	In ancient days, Shri Mahadeva at the destruction of Daksha's sacrifice, lifting up his bow in sport said to the gods: 'O Devas, you have failed to give me my share in the sacrifice, therefore, by means of this bow I shall destroy you all.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	"O Great Sage, the devas overwhelmed with fear, making supplication to the god, succeeded in propitiating Shri Mahadeva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	Then he delivered the bow to the gods and they bestowed it on King Devarata.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	This is the bow.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	"Thereafter, while I was ploughing the earth for a sacrifice, a virgin issued therefrom.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	Being uncovered by the edge of the plough, I named her Sita and she became my daughter.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	This earth-born virgin has grown up under my protection.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	For the marriage of my daughter, it was established by me and made known to the kings coming to seek her hand, that I should not bestow her on any prince whose strength had not been fully tried.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	O Renowned Sage, these kings have come to test their prowess and I have placed the bow before them and requested them to string it, but none as yet has been able to do so.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	Perceiving them to be deficient in strength, I have refused to bestow my daughter on any of them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	These kings, inflamed with anger, considering their failure to string the bow had brought them into disrepute, surrounded my capital, and inflicted great hardship on my people.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	This siege endured a full year and immeasurably reduced my treasury.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	Undergoing severe penances, I propitiated the gods, who granted me a large army with which I have defeated those kings who have retreated, bereft of courage, yet still smarting under imagined injury.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	"O Great Sage, this is that bow and I will show it to these two princes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	66_King Janaka relates the story of the great bow and the birth of Sita	O Rishi, should Shri Ramacandra be able to string the bow, I will give my daughter Sita to him in marriage."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	Hearing the words of King Janaka, Shri Vishvamitra said:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	"O King, let the bow be shown to Shri Rama."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	Then the monarch addressed his ministers, saying: "Go, bring the bow adorned with flowers and sandalwood, hither."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	The counsellors commanded by Janaka went to the capital and brought back the bow.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	Five hundred men, of great strength, brought the eight-wheeled cart on which the bow was placed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	Having brought the chest fashioned of iron containing the bow, the ministers addressed their divine sovereign, saying: "O Chief of Men, here is the bow worshipped by former kings.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	O Sovereign of Mithila, it is at your disposal."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	Then, with palms joined in humility, King Janaka spoke to the holy Sage Vishvamitra standing with Rama and Lakshmana: "O Holy Lord, this is the bow which has been the object of worship to the kings of the Nimi dynasty and which the monarchs of the earth coming hither have sought to string.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	Even the gods have not been able to raise, bend or string this bow.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	How, therefore, should mortals have the power to do so if the gods have failed?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	O Great Rishi, behold the bow, let the two princes examine it."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	The righteous Sage Vishvamitra, hearing the words of the king, said to Rama: "O Child, view this divine bow."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	Then Shri Rama, approaching the casket in which the bow lay, opened it and gazed upon it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	He said: "O Divine Lord, taking it in my hand and raising it up, I shall endeavour to string the bow."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	Then the king and the sage answered: "Be it so," and Shri Ramacandra with a slight effort, seizing the centre of the bow, lifted it up in the presence of thousands of people and without exertion drew it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	By the unparalleled strength of the illustrious Rama, the bow broke into two parts and a sound resembling the fall of a thunderbolt rang forth cleaving the mountains asunder and causing the earth to shake, and on this the people on every side fell insensible, save only Vishvamitra, Rama and Lakshmana.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	After a while, the people being somewhat restored, and the king's misgivings set at rest, he addressed the excellent Sage with humility, saying: "O Blessed Lord, I have witnessed the unparalleled, wonderful and incontestable feat of Shri Ramacandra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	My daughter, the Princess Sita, shall obtain Prince Rama as her lord and add to the glory of my dynasty.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	O Great Sage, to-day my pledge to subject the prospective wooer of my daughter to a trial of strength has been redeemed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	Now I shall bestow on Rama, Sita, who is dearer to me than my life.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	With your permission, O Sage, my messengers in swift chariots shall drive in all haste to Ayodhya and respectfully relating this event to King Dasaratha invite him to my capital.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	They shall further inform him regarding the well-being of the two princes protected by you and with due honour, convey the great king hither."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	67_Rama breaks the bow and is given the Princess Sita in marriage	The Sage Vishvamitra acquiescing to the proposal, the king communicated the matter to his messengers and entrusting them with a personal missive to King Dasaratha, sent them forth on their deputation.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	Commanded by King Janaka, the messengers in swift chariots, passing three nights on the way, their horses greatly fatigued, arrived at Ayodhya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	Entering the gates of the palace, they addressed the sentries, saying:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	"Please inform the king that we have come from King Janaka and desire an audience."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	King Dasaratha being informed, caused the messengers to be brought before him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	Entering the royal palace, they beheld the aged king who resembled a god.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	His benign and gracious presence putting them at their ease, they addressed him in gentle and submissive accents saying: "O Illustrious Sovereign, the Lord of the kingdom of Mithila, the performer of great sacrifices, King Janaka, enquires with affection as to your well-being and also concerning the welfare of your subjects.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	With the consent of the Sage Vishvamitra he sends you the following good tidings.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	His daughter who has been wooed by many kings unable to pass the requisite trial of strength, who have thereupon returned home discomfited, has been won by your highly fortunate and princely son.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	He, in the company of the Sage Vishvamitra, coming hither, broke the sacred bow in the presence of a great assembly, therefore, King Janaka desiring to see his daughter wedded to your son, Shri Ramacandra, sends you the following message: "O Great Sovereign be gracious enough to visit my kingdom with all speed, together with your preceptors, your family and attendants and be united with your sons.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	Accept the love I bear for you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	Do you come hither and witness the nuptials of your children.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	"O King, these are the words of King Janaka which we bring to you approved by the Sage Vishvamitra and the priest Shri Shatananda."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	Having uttered these words, the messengers, overawed by the sovereign's presence, became silent.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	On receiving these tidings, King Dasaratha full of joy, said to the holy Sage Vasishtha, Shri Vamadeva and his ministers: "Protected by Shri Vishvamitra, Shri Ramacandra and Prince Lakshmana are now in the city of Mithila.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	The renowned Janaka has witnessed the prowess of Shri Ramacandra and desires to give his daughter in marriage to him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	If this union is looked upon with favour by you, let us start for Mithila immediately, so that we may reach it with all speed."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	The sages and ministers there present, answered: "It is well," whereupon the king, highly pleased, said: "Let us set out to-morrow."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	68_King Janaka sends messengers to invite King Dasaratha to the capital	King Dasaratha with his counsellors entertained King Janaka's messengers with great respect, and they passed the night there in comfort.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	The night being over, King Dasaratha, glad in heart, accompanied by his spiritual preceptor and relations, summoned his chief minister, Sumantra, and said:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	"Let the officers of the treasury take with them wealth and jewels in abundance and precede us in good order.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Let the four divisions of my army hold themselves in readiness and let chariots and palanquins be prepared.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Let my commands be carried out with promptitude.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Suffer Shri Vasishtha, Vamadeva, Javali, Kashyapa, Bhrigu, Markandeya and Katya-yana with other learned and holy men to lead the procession.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Make ready the royal chariot, let there be no delay, King Janaka's messengers are eager to return."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Then the mighty King Dasaratha attended by the holy sages set out on the journey followed by his army.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Passing four nights on the road, they entered the capital of King Janaka, who, having commanded the city to be decorated, advanced to pay honour to his royal guests.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Approaching the aged sovereign Dasaratha, King Janaka was filled with joy, and addressed him with cheerful words, saying: "O Great King, I bid you welcome, fortunate indeed am I that you have been gracious enough to honour me with your presence.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Now shall you have the felicity of looking on your two sons.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Twice blessed am I that Shri Vasishtha, attended by other learned sages, has come hither also, as it were Indra in the midst of the gods.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Every impediment to the wedding ceremony has been withdrawn and this ancient dynasty, by the alliance with the House of Raghu, will acquire new lustre.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	O Illustrious Sovereign, to-morrow at the completion of the sacrifice, having consulted with the sages, be gracious enough to celebrate the nuptials."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	The eloquent monarch, Dasaratha, seated amidst the sages, answered: "I have ever heard that those who receive charity are subject to the conferrer of that charity!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	O You acquainted with virtue, it is ours to defer to you in all things."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	Hearing the speech of the truthful sovereign, King Dasaratha, King Janaka was filled with astonishment.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	All the sages then coming together, passed the night in converse, mutually delighting each other.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	King Dasaratha, being united with his sons was filled with happiness and surrendered himself wholly to King Janaka's hospitality.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	69_King Dasaratha sets out	The magnanimous sovereign of Mithila, having completed the orders for the preparations of the wedding ceremony, retired to rest.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The following day, King Janaka, having carried out the sacrifice with the assistance of the priests, said to Shri Shatananda:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	"My younger brother, the virtuous and mighty Kushadvaja, resides in the city of Sankamshya, which is surrounded by a moat and battlements, mounted by heavy batteries, the river Ikshu flowing at its side, and resembles the aerial chariot Pushpaka.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	I desire to see that Excellent One, who, with liberality, has assisted me in the act of sacrifice; it is meet that he should attend the marriage ceremony."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Having spoken thus to Shri Shatananda, certain attendants standing near, were commanded by the king to set out thither.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	At his command, the messengers, like gods riding out on the behest of Indra, went forth on swift horses to bring back the royal guest.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Arriving at Sankamshya, and being received by the King Kushadvaja, they acquainted him with King Janaka's proposal.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The great king acquiescing to his request, came to the capital of the sovereign of Mithila and beholding the virtuous great-souled Janaka, together with Shri Shatananda, bowed down to them in salutation.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Having occupied a royal seat in the assembly, the two illustrious brothers commanded their chief minister, Sudamana, saying: "O Chief of Counsellors, speedily approach the great sovereign, Dasaratha, of limitless glory, and bring that Excellent One to my court, together with the two princes and his ministers."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Sudamana, going to the encampment of King Dasaratha, and bowing down to him, said: "O Great Hero, O Lord of Ayodhya, the sovereign of Mithila humbly invites you with your spiritual preceptor, your priests and your two sons to his assembly."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Then King Dasaratha attended by his friends and kinsmen came to the place where King Janaka sat amidst the sages and ministers.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	And he, the wise and eloquent monarch addressed King Janaka, saying: "O Great King, it is known to you that the chief priest of the House of Ikshvaku is Shri Vasishtha and my spokesman in all matters.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Therefore, with the approval of Shri Vishvamitra he will relate the descent of our dynasty to you."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Having spoken, Dasaratha became silent and Shri Vasishtha then addressed King Janaka and Shri Shatananda:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	"From Brahman, the Unmanifest, the Eternal and Imperishable Brahma came forth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	From him was produced Marica, Marica begot Kashyapa; Kashyapa begot Surya, Surya begot Vivasvat, and Vivasvat begot Manu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Manu was the father of Ikswaku who was the first king of Ayodhya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The son of Ikswaku was Kukshi and his son was Vikukshi; the illustrious Vana was the son of Vikukshi and Vana's son was the mighty Anranya; his son was Prithu and the son of Prithu was Trishanku; the great Dhundhumara was the son of Trishanku and his son was the hero Yuvanashva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The renowned Mandhata was born of Yuvanashva and Mandhata's son was named Susandhi.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Susandhi had two sons Dhruvasandhi and Prasenajit.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Bharata was the son of Dhruvasandhi and the renowned Asit was the son of Bharata.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The three sons of Asit were Hihasas, Talajanghas and Shashavindus, great Kings, who, hostile to their sire, waged war against him and sent him into exile.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Then King Asit, with his two consorts, going to the Himalayas, there laid down his life, leaving the queens pregnant, whereat one of them, to destroy the fruit of the other's womb, gave her poison.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	"At that time, a sage of the family of Bhrigu dwelt on the heights of Himalaya, by name Cyavana practising penance there.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Then the lotus-eyed Queen Kalindi, desirous of bearing an excellent son approached the sage who resembled a god and bowed before him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The brahmin addressed the queen saying:
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	'O Fortunate One, you bearest in your womb, a hero, soon to be born together with the poison; have no anxiety.'
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	"The queen, faithful to her deceased lord, overcome with sorrow, fearing the death of her child, paid homage to the muni.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Thereafter she bore a son, born with the poison administered by the other wife and he was named Sagara.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	"The son of Sagara was Asumanjas, and his son was Amshuman.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The son of Amshuman was Dilipa, and Dilipa's son was Bhagiratha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The son of Bhagiratha was Kakustha and his son was Raghu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The son of Raghu, Prabradha became a demon, and was subsequently called Kalamashapada and his son was Shangana.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The son of Shangana was Sudarshana, and his son was Agnivarna.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Shighraga was the son of Agnivarna and the son of Shighraga was Manu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Manu's son was Prashushruka and his son was Ambarisha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	Ambarisha's son was named Nahusha and his son was Yayati.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	The son of Yayati was Nabhaga.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	"The son of Nabhaga was Aja, and the son of Aja was King Dasaratha; the two sons of King Dasaratha are Rama and Lakshmana.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	"O King, I have recounted the genealogy of King Ikswaku to you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	All these kings were noble, virtuous and distinguished in their love of truth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	"King Dasaratha requests the hands of your daughters in marriage for his two sons, who are in every way worthy to be your kinsmen.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	70_Vishvamitra relates the descent of the dynasty	O Chief of Men, bestow your daughters on them."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	King Janaka, paying homage to the Sage Vasishtha, said: "O Maharishi, be peace with you, hear the account of the succession of our dynasty.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	At the time of bestowing a daughter in marriage, it is customary for the father to recite the pedigree of his race, be gracious enough to hear me, O Lord.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	"In ancient times, renowned in the three worlds was the King Nimi, eminent in virtue, a lover of truth and foremost among kings of that era.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	Nimi begot Mithi whose son was the first Janaka and he begot Udavasu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	His son was Nandivardhana and he begot Suketu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	Suketu begot the righteous Devarata and the son of Devarata was the royal Sage Brihadratha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	He begot the great hero Mahavirya whose son was Dhratiman and his son was the truthful Sudhriti.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	He begot Dhrishta-Ketu and his son was the royal Sage Haryashva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	Haryashva begot Maru.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	Then followed Prasidhaka, Kirttiratha, Devamirha, Bibudha, Mahidhraka, Kirtivaja and Maharoma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	Maharoma begot Svarnaroma and his son was Hrasvaroma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	Hrasvaroma had two sons of whom I, myself, am the elder, and this is my younger brother Kushadvaja.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	My father, bequeathing the kingdom to me and charging me with the care of Kushadvaja, retired to the forest.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	My aged sire, having passed from this world, I began to rule according to dharma, supporting my brother with the utmost affection.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	After some time, the King Sudhanva besieged the capital of Mithila, thereafter he sent me offers of peace on condition I surrendered my daughter, Sita, and also the sacred bow of Shiva to him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	O Brahmarishi, on rejecting his offer a battle ensued between us in which Sudhanva was slain.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	O Great Sage, King Sudhanva being dead, I gave the kingdom of Sankasya to my well-beloved brother Kushadvaja.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	This is my well-beloved brother.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	O Sages, we submit ourselves in love, to you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	"O Raghava, to Shri Ramacandra I give my daughter Sita, and Prince Lakshmana will receive the Princess Urmila.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	Sita, resembling a daughter of the gods, I bestow on Rama; verily with my whole heart do I yield these two daughters of mine to your sons.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	O King, now be pleased to inaugurate the traditional distribution of kine in charity.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	Perform the Nandi-Mukha ceremony so that the nuptials may be celebrated.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	"To-day the Magda star is in die ascendant and in three days the Uttara Phalguni will have risen; the marriage should take place in that conjunction.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	71_King Janaka gives an account of the succession and his dynasty	"For the purpose of ensuring their felicity, let Rama and Lakshmana now distribute cows, land, sesamum seed and other requisite offerings."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	King Janaka having uttered these words, Mahamuni Vishvamitra, as desired by Shri Vasishtha, said to him:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	"O King, wonderful indeed are the two Houses of Ikshvaku and Videha, their glory is limitless, verily they have no equal.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	Shri Rama and Sita are in perfect accord one with the other, as also Lakshmana and Urmila, each equals the other in grace and heritage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	O Virtuous King, I have something further to say, hear me.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	Your younger brother, King Kushadvaja, unexcelled in virtue, has two daughters of incomparable beauty, these two I request for the sagacious Bharata and the pious Shatrughna.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	The four sons of King Dasaratha are youthful, handsome, resembling the gods, equal to the (four) guardians of the world.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	O Great King, bestow these two damsels on the younger sons of King Dasaratha.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	You are unequalled in virtue and the House of Ikswaku is without a peer."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	Hearing the magnanimous words of Shri Vishvamitra echoed by Shri Vasishtha, King Janaka with joined palms humbly addressed the two august sages:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	"O Holy Ones, I am proud that you have approved the alliance of my House with the House of Ikshvaku.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	Your commands shall be accomplished.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	The daughters of King Kushadvaja shall be given to the Princes Bharata and Shatrughna in marriage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	Let the four great sons of King Dasaratha be united with the four princesses on the same day.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	O Divine Sage, to-morrow the constellation Phalguni presided over by the deity Bhag [one of the Adityas q.v.,] is in the ascendant.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	The wise consider this season as auspicious for the nuptials."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	Shri Vasishtha answering "Be it so", King Janaka, in great humility, addressed the holy sages, saying: "O Spiritual Kings, it is by your favour that I am able to offer my daughters in marriage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	Regard me as your servant.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	You are worthy of these seats prepared for you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	Let my kingdom now belong to the King Dasaratha and my affections extend to the kingdom of Ayodhya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	I have spoken truth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	O Holy Ones, do what is considered necessary."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	King Dasaratha hearing with attention the words uttered by King Janaka was pleased and replied, saying: "O Brothers, possessing innumerable excellent qualities, you have honoured the holy rishis and kings with abundant hospitality.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	May you be blessed I May happiness be yours!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	With your leave I shall now withdraw to my own apartments to inaugurate the preliminary rites."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	Having taken leave of the King of Mithila, Shri Dasaratha, preceded by the holy sage, went away.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	The following day, having fulfilled the traditional rites, King Dasaratha gave away innumerable cows in charity.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	On behalf of each of his sons, he bestowed on the brahmins thousands of cows whose horns were covered with gold, yielding rich milk, together with their calves.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	With every cow the king gave away a metal milking vessel.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	On that day, four hundred thousand cows were given away by him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	That mighty king holding his sons supremely dear, gave incalculable wealth in their name.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	72_The marriage of the four sons of King Dasaratha	King Dasaratha, performing these deeds of charity, surrounded by his sons, resembled Brahma attended by the Regents of the world.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	On the day on which King Dasaratha distributed the cows in charity, the great hero Yudhajit, the son of the King Kaikeya and the maternal uncle of Bharata, also came to Janaka's capital.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Seeing King Dasaratha, he made enquiries as to his welfare and said: "O King, the Lord of Kaikeya, through affection, sends tidings of his well-being to you, and seeks to know if it be well with your friends.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	O Great King, my father desired to see Prince Bharata, and for this purpose I went to Ayodhya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	There, hearing that you had gone to Mithila with your sons, for their nuptials, I came hither in haste to see the son of my sister."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	King Dasaratha thereupon duly honoured his kinsman who spent the night happily in company with the princes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	The following day, rising early, King Dasaratha performing his customary devotions, proceeded to the sacrificial pavilion, escorted by the sages.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	At an auspicious hour in the presence of Shri Vasishtha and other sages, Shri Ramacandra and his brothers adorned with every ornament being present, the preliminary ceremonies were performed.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Then Shri Vasishtha addressed King Janaka saying: "O King, King Dasaratha has inaugurated the preliminary ceremonies, he now awaits your pleasure.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	The sacred rite is completed when host and guests come together.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Be pleased, therefore, to perform the principal nuptial rites."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	King Janaka listened to the words of the great-souled Vasishtha and answered: "What guard detains King Dasaratha at the gate?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Whose sanction does his royal majesty seek?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Is not this his house?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Let the king enter!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	O Chief of Sages, my daughters, in readiness, stand at the altar, bright as the clear flame.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	I, standing near, await you all.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	There is no need for delay.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Let the king cause the ceremony to take place without further hindrance."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Then King Dasaratha with his sons and the holy sages entered the marriage pavilion.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Thereafter, King Janaka addressed Shri Vasishtha, saying: "O Virtuous Sage, with the other sages perform the wedding ceremony."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Then Shri Vasishtha ignited the sacrificial fire in the centre of the pavilion.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Shri Vishvamitra and Shri Shatananda standing before him, sprinkled the altar with perfume, and decorated it with flowers.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Then he set out the golden vessels and the sacred kusha grass, filling many pots with incense and arranging them in the form of a conchshell.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Dishes filled with parched com and rice were placed there, and durbha grass spread about, the sacred formulas being pronounced over them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	The holy rishis now lit a fire pronouncing the Vedic mantrams and offered oblations into it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Shri Sita, adorned with jewels, took her seat by the sacred fire opposite Shri Ramacandra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	King Janaka, addressing the Son of Raghu, said: "O Rama, from to-day my daughter Sita will be your companion in virtue.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Accept her, O Prince, and take her hand in thine.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	This fortunate princess, faithful and tender, will constantly attend you, following you like a shadow, in loving obedience.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	May you both be happy."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Saying this, King Janaka sprinkled on them water purified by mantrams.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Then all the gods cried, "Jai!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Jai!"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	and divine music sounded, while a shower of flowers fell from the skies.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Thus was Sita joined in marriage to Shri Ramacandra.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Then King Janaka said to Shri Lakshmana: "O Lakshmana, come hither, peace be with you!
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Take in your hand the hand of my daughter Urmila, tarry not, O Prince."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Having thus spoken, Janaka likewise addressed Prince Bharata, saying: "O Son of Raghu, accept the hand of the Princess Mandavi" and to Prince Shatrughna, he said: "O Great Prince, accept the hand of Shruta-kirtti.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	O Princes of the House of Raghu, be gentle and faithful to your wives as they will be to you, receive them now, let there be no delay."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Thus instructed by King Janaka, the four princes, taking the hands of the four princesses as directed by the Sage Vasishtha, circumambulated the fire, King Janaka and the sages performing the rites as ordained by the sacred ordinance.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	As the nuptial ceremony of the four princes of the House of Raghu with the four princesses terminated, a rain of flowers fell on them from the sky.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Divine music sounded, nymphs danced and the celestial singers broke into paeons of praise.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	All these marvellous events marked the wedding of the sons of King Dasaratha while the princes, circumambulating the fire, were united with their brides.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	73_The marriage ceremonies are completed	Thereafter with their wives, they returned to their apartments and King Janaka with his relatives and friends, with a joyful heart having taken part in the festivities, also withdrew.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	The night being past, the great Sage Vishvamitra took leave of King Dasaratha and King Janaka and, blessing the princes and their sire, departed for the Himalayas to meditate there.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	The holy rishi being gone, King Dasaratha begged the permission of the Lord of Mithila to return to his capital.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	Bidding farewell to the pious king, Janaka escorted him for some distance on his way.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	To the King of Ayodhya, on behalf of his daughter, King Janaka gave a hundred thousand cows, woollen cloths, countless silken robes and richly decorated elephants, horses and chariots.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	He also bestowed on him male and female attendants, numberless golden coins with quantities of pearls and coral.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	All these and many other gifts King Janaka gave with a joyful mind, and having taken leave of King Dasaratha, returned to Mithila, whereupon King Dasaratha with his illustrious sons, preceded by the sages, started on the homeward journey, accompanied by his army.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	As the sages, with Shri Ramacandra, advanced in company with the king, the screeching of strange and terrible birds was heard, while frightened deer fled across their path.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	Perceiving these inauspicious signs, the king addressed Shri Vasishtha, saying: "O Holy Guru, why do the birds cry thus ominously, and the deer traverse our path?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	What do these omens portend?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	My mind is filled with anxiety, O Divine Lord."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	The Maharishi Vasishtha, in gentle tones, replied: "O King, the fearful crying of the birds betokens some great danger, but the crossing of the deer from left to right indicates a speedy end to your fears."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	While they were yet speaking, the earth began to quake and and giant trees fell down, darkness covered the earth and clouds of dust veiled the sun, nor could the cardinal points be discerned.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	In the great dust storm that followed, the army was overwhelmed with terror and all became paralysed, save Shri Vasishtha, King Dasaratha and the princes alone.
