RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	When the dust was allayed and the army somewhat recovered, Shri Vasishtha beheld the son of Yamadagni of dreadful aspect.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	With matted hair, Parasurama, the humbler of the pride of kings and emperors, drew near.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	The appearance of the muni resembling the splendour of Mount Kailasha or the fires of dissolution at the end of the world-period was hardly to be borne by human eyes.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	With his battle axe on his shoulder, bearing a mighty bow, brilliant as lightning, he appeared like Shiva about to strike down Tripura.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	Beholding Parasurama resembling a blazing fire, the sages reflected among themselves and said: "His father being slain, has Parasurama come again to destroy the warrior caste?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	Was not his anger appeased when he formerly destroyed the whole warrior caste?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	Has he come again to take his revenge on us?"
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	Reflecting thus, they approached Parasurama with traditional offerings, saying: "O Rama, accept this arghya."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	74_Parasurama appears amidst inauspicious signs	Shri Parasurama accepting the offering, then addressed Shri Rama.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	"O Rama, O Illustrious Hero, I have heard of your great prowess.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	I have also been acquainted with your heroic deed, the breaking of the bow at Janakapura, verily a feat exciting wonder and surpassing imagination.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	Having heard of thine achievement, I, taking this other bow, have come hither.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	With this terrible bow named Yamadagni, show your strength, O Rama, and placing an arrow in it, discharge it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	Should'st you be able to accomplish this, I will engage in honourable combat with you."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	Hearing these words, King Dasaratha, became dejected and humbly addressed the rishi, saying: "O Holy Parasurama, you are a great brahmin sage, it becomes you not to show anger to warriors; be gracious unto my son, who is still a child.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	You are born in the family of Bhrigu and hast pledged thyself to Indra to bear arms no more.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	Having given the dominion of the world to Kashyapa and retired to the Mahendra mountain to practise asceticism, why hast you now come hither to destroy us?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	O Sage, if Rama is slain, none of us will survive."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	The great son of Jamadagni, disregarding the entreaty of King Dasaratha, again addressed Rama, saying: "O Rama, these two bows of exquisite design, famed throughout the world, exceedingly powerful, were forged by Vishvakarma.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	One of them, wielded by Shri Shiva in combat with Tripura, was broken by you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	The other, held by me, of inexpressible power, was given to Vishnu by the gods and is known to give victory over the foe; it is equal in moment to that which you have broken.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	"Formerly the gods asked Brahma which of the two excelled the other and Shri Brahma, acquainted with their intention, invoked a quarrel between Vishnu and Mahadeva.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	They entered into combat one with the other.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	By the shout raised by Shri Vishnu, Shri Mahadeva was struck motionless and his bow unstrung.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	Then the gods and rishis came to that place and caused the two gods to be reconciled.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	Thereafter the gods esteemed the bow of Vishnu to be the more powerful and Shri Shiva surrendered his bow to the King of Mithila, together with all its arrows.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	"This bow, belonging to Vishnu, was given in ancient times by that god to Richika and he gave it to his son Jamadagni, my father.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	He having renounced the bearing of weapons, retired to practise austerity, when the rash and foolish monarch Sahasravaku slew him.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	Hearing of the cruel death of my sire, I successively destroyed the warrior caste, from generation to generation, thus acquiring dominion over the earth.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	I conferred this great dominion as a gift on the Sage Kashyapa at the completion of a sacrifice, and retired to the Mahendra mountain, cheerfully observing the practice of Yoga.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	To-day, O Valiant Prince, acquainted with your great achievement, I have come hither to behold you.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	Receive this bow, bestowed on my ancestors by Shri Vishnu and in the spirit of a warrior, place an arrow on it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	75_Parasurama challenges Rama to combat	If you succeed in drawing the bow, I will challenge you to fight."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	Hearing these words, Shri Rama having regard for the presence of his sire, answered with restraint, saying: "O Parasurama, your deeds are known to me, as also the avenging of your fathers' murderers.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	Methinks you dost deem me lacking in valour, I, a kshatriya, and a descendant of the Solar race.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	O Rishi, witness my prowess."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	Having spoken thus, Shri Ramacandra, incensed, seized the bow and arrows from the rishi's hands and stringing it, placed an arrow on it.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	While drawing the mighty bow, the son of Dasaratha addressed the rishi with defiance, saying: "O Sage, you are a brahmin and as such do I honour you; you are further a kinsman of Shri Vishvamitra, therefore I shall not slay you with this arrow, but by this shaft I will rob you of the power of motion so that you shall no longer be able to travel through space, or I will banish you from those high regions to which you have attained by the practice of penance.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	Say, what is your desire?
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	This divine arrow of Vishnu, possessing the power of vanquishing the strength and pride of the foe, may not be restored by me to the quiver, till it has accomplished its great purpose."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	When Rama placed the arrow in the sacred bow, Brahma, with the gods, assembled to behold that glorious deed, followed by the gandharvas, apsaras, yakshas and other beings.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	Shri Ramacandra, having taken up the mighty bow, the three worlds began to tremble and Parasurama, bereft of his divine power, stood aghast.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	Deprived of his glory and powerless, Shri Parasurama with humble entreaty, addressed the lotus-eyed Rama:--
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	"When the dominion of the earth was given by me to the sage Kashyapa, he said 'You must not inhabit this kingdom Therefore, O Rama, in obedience to the sage, I do not stay on the earth by night.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	This world is no longer mine, but belongs to Kashyapa.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	O Rama, do not deprive me of the power of movement, but allow me speedily to return to the beautiful Mahendra mountain.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	You can'st deprive me of the merits earned by the practice of Yoga.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	I know You to be the Imperishable, You are verily Vishnu Himself, none but You could'st wield this bow.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	O Son of Raghu, the gods have assembled to behold You; You are pre-eminent in combat, and the conqueror of Thine enemies.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	O Virtuous Prince, to be defeated by You is no ignominy; discharge Your matchless arrow and I will return to the Mahendra mountain."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	Thereupon Shri Ramacandra discharged the arrow and the merit of Parasurama was rendered void, whereupon he speedily departed to the Mahendra mountain.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	76_Parasurama is vanquished and deprived of his glory and power	The darkness being dispelled and the whole world once more filled with light, Rama was worshipped by the gods and rishis, and Shri Parasurama having circumambulated the son of Dasaratha, returned to his own hermitage.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Shri Parasurama having departed, Shri Rama delivered the bow and arrows as a trust to the god Varuna.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Having offered salutations to Shri Vasishtha and the other sages he, seeing his father filled with apprehension, addressed him, saying: "Sire, Shri Parasurama has now gone, do you command thine army to proceed towards Ayodhya."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	King Dasaratha, hearing Rama's words, embraced him and reflected that his son was born to him a second time.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Then summoning his army to advance, he in a chariot, adorned with banners, to the fanfare of trumpets proclaiming victory, entered Ayodhya.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	The streets of the city sprinkled with water and flowers, appeared beautiful, and the citizens rejoicing at the return of their sovereign, greeted him with shouts of welcome.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Met by the brahmins inhabiting the city, the king with his friends and relatives, followed by the princes and their brides, entered the royal palace which was white as snow.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	There, the kindred of the king welcomed him with garlands and sandalwood.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	The Queens Kaushalya, Sumitra and Kaikeyi received the brides and conducted the fortunate Sita, the illustrious Urmila, and the two daughters of Kushadvaj [Kushadvaja] to their palace, with auspicious rites.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Arrayed in sumptuous silken robes, and borne to the temple to worship the holy images, the brides then offered respectful salutations to their mother-in-laws, and others worthy of honour.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Thereafter, each began to live with her lord in her own palace.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Shri Ramacandra with the other princes, possessing the knowledge of the use of weapons and the science of defence, passed the time with their friends in attendance on their aged sire.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	After some time, King Dasaratha said to his son Bharata: "O my Son, your maternal uncle, who came for the purpose of taking you to his home, still tarries in the capital, therefore, go with him to see your grandfather."
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Prince Bharata and Prince Shatrughna prepared to start on their journey and took leave of their father and their highly compassionate brother Rama.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Bharata being gone, Shri Rama and Lakshmana ministered to the aged king as if he were a god and in his name performed charitable deeds among the people of the city.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Rama also ministered to his mother with deep affection, and served his Guru with single-minded devotion.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	His noble behaviour gratified the king, the brahmins, merchants and other castes; his sweet disposition and pious conduct charmed the people of the capital.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Rama, wholly devoted to truth was renowned for his virtue, and endowed with every excellent quality like Swayambhu Brahma himself.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	For a long time did Shri Rama enjoy a life of content with Sita.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	To him, she was dear beyond all things and he surrendered his whole heart to her.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Love is enhanced by beauty, virtue and gentleness, and Sita possessed all these in an equal degree with Rama.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	Lovely as a goddess, Shri Sita was able to discern the thoughts of her lord before he expressed them.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	The beautiful Sita with Shri Ramacandra wholly satisfied, resembled Lakshmi, the consort of the incomparable Vishnu.
RAMA	01_Bala-kanda	77_King Dasaratha returns to Ayodhya	END OF BALA KANDA.
